# UDT Mass Codex — Codex Working Instructions

Charles canonizes. Nothing enters `CANON.md` without his explicit sign-off.
This repository is an evidence ledger, not a place to turn a promising lead into a stronger claim.

## Mandatory startup

Work on branch `grok`. Do not trust a hash, branch count, or status quoted in a prompt or handoff.
At the start of every fresh session run, in order:

```bash
git checkout grok
git fetch origin
git pull --ff-only origin grok
git status --short --branch
git log -8 --oneline
```

If a pull is blocked by local work, preserve and inspect that work. Never reset, overwrite, clean, or
stash user changes merely to make the pull succeed. If an untracked file collides with an identical
upstream file, prove that it is byte-identical and preserve a backup before moving it aside.

Before interpreting the frontier, read from disk in this exact order. **Bounded-startup rule:** do
not dump whole long files or recursively open every cited artifact during orientation. Read only the
marked/current sections below; expand to full reports, scripts, JSON, logs, or historical layers only
after the user's actual task makes them load-bearing.

1. `LIVE.md` — read only the range between `STARTUP_CURRENT_BEGIN` and `STARTUP_CURRENT_END`; its
   `CURRENT STATE` overrides every other status description. Do not read the remaining historical
   layers at startup.
2. `HANDOFF.md` — read only its `STARTUP_CURRENT_BEGIN` / `STARTUP_CURRENT_END` range.
3. `UDT_SCIENTIFIC_FRONTIER_2026-07-19.md` — initially read only `Current honest result`, `Current
   open discriminator`, and `Authority boundary`.
4. `angular_toric_closure_selector_2026-07-19/LAY_DECISION_TREE.md`, then
   `angular_toric_closure_selector_2026-07-19/STATUS_LEDGER.tsv` — the compact current theorem,
   counterfamily boundary, and two ordered gates. Read the full package `AUDIT_REPORT.md` only when
   the task requires its derivation or provenance.
5. `null_section_hopfion_metric_audit_2026-07-19/AUDIT_REPORT.md` only when the exact reciprocal
   Hopf-orbit witness or its provenance becomes load-bearing, then
   `native_hopfion_topology_audit_2026-07-19/AUDIT_REPORT.md` for the preceding carrier/topology
   classification only when that layer is relevant.
6. The exact scripts plus JSON/NPZ/log outputs load-bearing for the current return or task; none are
   part of generic startup orientation.
7. `stability_branch_follow_256_DECISION.md` when particle operator/stability history is relevant; it
   is durable lane evidence, not the global frontier.
8. `CLAUDE.md` sections `How we work`, `DRIVER TRIGGERS`, and repo discipline only; do not dump the
   whole charter at startup.
9. Only the specific full protocol under `.claude/skills/*/SKILL.md` triggered by the actual task;
   do not preload every skill.
10. The top/current summary in `INDEX.md` and `MEMORY.md`'s `TOP — CURRENT POINTER` for pointers only;
    neither can overrule `LIVE.md`.

For the 1,114 fixed-base artifact identities, use
`research/_registry/CURRENT_ARTIFACT_PATHS.tsv`. Post-base additions such as the July 19 frontier and
audit packages are outside that fixed universe; use their direct tracked paths named by `LIVE.md`
rather than expecting registry rows. The R0–R1C ownership, readiness, census, preregistration, and
verification records are fixed historical snapshots and must not be rewritten to mimic current
paths. This is an operational navigation rule; like every instruction in this file, it cannot
overrule `LIVE.md`.

Then give Charles a short orientation report: actual HEAD and dirt, the current honest claim, its
premise stamps, the open gate, and the proposed bounded next action. Do not mutate files or launch a
long solve until that orientation is complete.

The bootstrap/stable-matter interpretation remains a working hypothesis. The bounded audit chain is
complete through angular–toric closure: the existing implementation is already full 3D Hopf-capable;
the reciprocal metric has an exact conditional Hopf-orbit-block witness; and `S3` plus free
diagonal/anti-diagonal Hopf actions are unique only after global toric eigencap premises are supplied.
Registered UDT does not yet derive the first missing gate—transverse spatial reciprocal realization
and periodicity—or the conditional second gate of finite-cell cap completion. Do not silently turn
either conditional theorem, the earlier celestial fiber, or the time-live proposal into authority to
adopt a carrier, section, torus, cap, framing, boundary, dynamical completion, run GPU work, or claim
a bootstrap parameter-selection theorem.

## Codex/Claude compatibility

`CLAUDE.md` and `.claude/skills/` contain binding project method even though their names are
Claude-specific. Read and apply them manually when their trigger applies. Codex must not assume that
`.claude/hooks/corral_trigger.py`, Claude project memory, background jobs, or Claude skill auto-loading
are active. The corresponding pauses are therefore manual and mandatory:

- before a solve: observing or targeting; whole frame or bounded slice; every physical choice tagged;
- before explaining a mismatch: solver completeness before any new mechanism;
- before a commit or verdict: preregistration, bounded scope, independent verification of the
  load-bearing premise, and premise audit;
- before words such as *proved*, *settled*, *stable*, *single basin*, *native*, or *derived*: state the
  exact regime and the remaining open scope.

Do not rely on conversational memory. Disk evidence wins.

## Binding UDT research rules

- Remain pure to UDT: **the metric is the theory**.
- Trace every claimed result explicitly to the UDT metric and the stated matter carrier.
- Keep the macro WR-L lane separate from the particle-mass/carrier lane.
- Do not import Lambda-CDM, Standard Model physics, quantum mechanics, QED, GR field equations,
  fluids, Q-balls, boson stars, or textbook mechanisms as UDT derivations. They may be comparison or
  readout tools only, clearly labeled.
- The `S^2` carrier is a `POSIT`, not a derived necessity. A replacement or emergence remains open.
- The conditional conformal-Lorentzian null-direction fiber is a celestial topological/conformal
  `S^2`; it does not by itself derive the carrier's fixed round target, section, transport, action,
  or boundary completion.
- An EH metric-only action is `CONDITIONAL` through the stated minimality premise; it is not native UDT
  merely because it is mathematically familiar.
- No fitting, fudge factors, hard physical cutoffs, effective corrections, or invented couplings.
- Numerical controls and consistent discretizations are allowed only when they do not change the
  tested continuum functional.
- Use full nonlinear covariant operators. Do not linearize without a controlled error and an explicit
  scope stamp.
- Audit algebra, signs, boundary conditions, operator provenance, convergence, raw evidence, and code
  before accepting or abandoning an approach.
- Use the labels `DERIVED`, `CHOSE`, `WORKING`, `OPEN`, `CONDITIONAL`, `POSIT`, and `OBSERVED`
  precisely. A numerical result is `OBSERVED`, not automatically physics or canon.
- Raw residual/backward error remains the certification gate. A preconditioned residual may diagnose
  or accelerate, but never silently replace it.

## Method

Default order is `MAP -> OBSERVE -> PONDER -> DERIVE`. MAP and PONDER with Charles are brief and in lay
language. Derivation begins only after the frame, assumptions, and premise ledger are visible and
Charles gives the go.

For every proposed computation, state:

1. the whole question and the exact bounded regime being sampled;
2. whether the question is metric-led or template-led;
3. every physical value, boundary condition, sign, chart, source, carrier, and action premise as
   `free-and-explored`, `pinned-by-THEORY` with a citation, or `pinned-by-HABIT`;
4. what degrees of freedom, sectors, branches, boundaries, and limits are not covered;
5. a preregistered falsification/certification contract and maximum allowed conclusion.

Characterize the solution space; do not filter it to demand a particle, lump, spectrum, smooth shape,
or expected answer. A negative is always premise-scoped. If a premise changes, re-grade every negative
that depended on it.

When a result disagrees with expectation, check in order: omitted terms/sectors/boundaries, numerical
convergence or bugs, frozen degrees of freedom, and incomplete solution-space exploration. Do not add a
mechanism to repair a mismatch.

## Evidence and banking

- Pre-register tests, tolerances, candidates, classifications, and conclusion wording before seeing
  outcomes. Do not retune after inspection.
- Independently recompute the load-bearing quantity from saved artifacts. Hunt circular checks,
  shared-code false independence, vacuous assertions, loose tolerances, and incomplete sampling.
- For a load-bearing result, use a fresh adversarial context and an independent implementation; use a
  different method or model family where practical. A same-code comparison is a regression check, not
  independent evidence.
- Preserve raw stdout/stderr, compact machine-readable outputs, exact commands, versions, parameters,
  array shapes, and SHA-256 manifests for large artifacts.
- Commit one logical evidence change at a time and push `grok`. Edit the canonical live file rather
  than proliferating `v2` scripts; git is the rollback trail.
- Do not edit `LIVE.md` or `CANON.md` unless the current dispatch or Charles explicitly authorizes it.
  Never overwrite grid artifacts; use grid-tagged and branch-tagged filenames.
- Preserve unrelated dirty and untracked files. Never use destructive git or filesystem commands.

Before banking any verdict, explicitly report the four gates:

1. preregistered;
2. full space, or bounded scope justified;
3. independently verified on the load-bearing premise;
4. every premise audited.

If any gate is absent, bank a `LEAD`, `OPEN`, or `VERIFIED-WITH-CAVEATS`, not a settled result.

## Numerical operations

- Use one GPU process at a time. Confirm the selected process, device, dtype, grid, memory estimate,
  output names, timeout, checkpoint/restart behavior, and stop conditions before launch.
- Prefer saved-field recomputation to repeating a relaxation.
- Bound exploratory work. Long production work requires a written dispatch and preregistered gates.
- Check GPU results with independent CPU/symbolic anchors where feasible.
- For corrected-carrier work, use the audited no-null `L2+L4` functional and its exact-HVP path; old
  centered-derivative tools are provenance only unless a task explicitly audits them.
- A relaxation trajectory is not physical time evolution. A finite box is not the infinite-volume
  limit. Positive sampled Ritz values alone are not stability certification.

## Communication

Keep returns concise but retain decisive equations and raw gates. Lead with what was actually learned,
then state what remains open. Separate observation, inference, and canonization. Charles owns the final
physics verdict.

# Verdict: FAIL

The package’s `COMPLETE_VERIFIED_WITH_CAVEATS` grade and four “YES” evidence gates are not justified. This does not refute the underlying conditional toric/Hopf algebra; it fails the package’s verification claim.

## Blocking findings

1. **A preregistered covariance gate was never exercised.** The contract requires projector matching under coordinate transformations ([PREREGISTRATION.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/PREREGISTRATION.md:164)). Neither current verifier transforms the path projectors or their derivatives. Moreover, Frobenius and convergence thresholds use Euclidean component norms ([build_correspondence_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/build_correspondence_atlas.py:227)), which are chart-dependent. The Frobenius tensor formula itself is valid, but its numerical certification is only for the registered chart.

2. **The claimed independent toric verification is circular.** Production hard-codes the Hessian eigentuples and a standard Hopf map ([derive_toric_control.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/derive_toric_control.py:31)); the independent verifier hard-codes the same formulas rather than deriving them from the metric ([verify_correspondence_independent.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_correspondence_independent.py:283)). The production script hashes `fs_hopfion.py` but never reads or compares its `hopf_seed` implementation. Therefore the report’s “exact independent toric” statement ([AUDIT_REPORT.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md:185)) is unsupported by its packaged verifier.

3. **The catch proofs are largely assertions about declared fields, not mutation tests.** Several independent catches are tautologies such as `len(ids[:-1]) != 64`; package catches directly throw an `AssertionError` rather than pass corrupted evidence through the validator ([verify_package.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_package.py:84)). Thus “11/11” and “13/13 catches” overstates validator strength.

4. **Carrier/action accounting is internally contradictory.** The connection and quotient use a supplied equal-weight diagonal action, yet the result records `construction_used_carrier_or_action: false` ([derive_toric_control.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/derive_toric_control.py:90)). The package verifier enforces that false boolean while separately requiring the action-premise string. The report’s prose correctly calls the action supplied, but the machine catch does not audit import.

5. **“Coherent projector bundles” exceeds the sampled evidence.** Stability means equal motif at 17 nodes with matchable labels; it has no continuity-distance gate ([build_correspondence_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/build_correspondence_atlas.py:418)). Among paths labelled stable, 70 have maximum adjacent component distance above `0.5`, 33 above `1`, and the maximum is `6.57`. A 257-node replay of the worst path retained its motif, so this is not a found counterexample, but the evidence supports sampled continuation—not a continuous bundle theorem or independently verified endpoint transport.

## Checks that did pass

- Both requested verifiers completed and reproduced their banked `PASS_WITH_CAVEATS` outputs byte-for-byte. They were run in a temporary mirror because they write result files; I made no worktree edits.
- All declared frozen manifests and their contents passed SHA-256 checks, including the transitively pinned amplitude-volume and joint-invariant sources.
- All path, summary, and distribution primary keys are unique. Threshold labels match their stored values.
- The Frobenius projector formula has the correct tensor index structure. Nonintegrable rows are well separated in the registered chart: minimum `9.73e-4` versus the `1e-5` gate. Integrable maximum is `5.16e-8`; one row remains uncertain.
- The `8,370` four-line rows are six distinct rank-two planes per midpoint, not duplicate keys. However, the `1+1+2` atlas semantically repeats its primitive rank-two plane as one complementary-split side—8,205 extra diagnostic rows. The report’s headline `6,669/1,536` uses only primitive rows, so it is not inflated by this.
- Open paths are correctly marked `NOT_TESTED_BY_OPEN_PATH`; no holonomy is claimed.
- No local-to-global Hopf promotion occurs. Periodicity, action, caps, orientation, and normalization remain explicit supplied premises.
- No seed-to-relaxed-field identity is claimed ([AUDIT_REPORT.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md:161)).

## Independent toric/seed result

I independently derived the Christoffels and mixed Hessian from the stated metric. They reproduce

\[
H^\mu{}_\nu=
\operatorname{diag}\!\left(
0,-A'/A^3,\frac{\Omega'/\Omega-1}{A^2},
\frac{\Omega'/\Omega+1}{A^2}
\right),
\]

the angular gap \(2/A^2\), and the \(\Omega\)-independent connection after supplying \(K=\partial_{\xi_1}+\partial_{\xi_2}\). A direct 1,000-point comparison with the checked-in inverse-stereographic [`hopf_seed`](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/hopfion_arc_scripts_2026-07-05/fs_hopfion.py:19) agreed to \(1.1\times10^{-14}\).

Thus the exact seed-level identity is true, but it is a template/action-conditioned compatibility witness, not a metric selection or carrier derivation.

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_FIXED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS`

plus

# Adversarial-review correction preregistration

Date: 2026-07-22

Parent evidence state: `72ede1ab88b692c14b709b2e00626d41eb90c67e` plus the unbanked production
outputs reviewed in `FRESH_ADVERSARIAL_REVIEW_RAW.md`.

The fresh review returned `FAIL` for the draft package grade. The numerical census is retained as
candidate evidence, but `COMPLETE_VERIFIED_WITH_CAVEATS`, all four affirmative evidence gates, and
the phrase “coherent projector bundles” are withdrawn before banking. This correction may restore
only claims supported by the tests below; it may not erase or rewrite the failed review.

## Registered defects

1. The registered nonlinear-coordinate projector covariance gate was not exercised in this package.
2. Frobenius obstruction values use component Euclidean norms and therefore certify only the
   registered chart unless a separate transformation test is added.
3. The packaged toric check repeated production formulas instead of deriving them from the metric,
   and it did not execute or directly compare the checked-in `hopf_seed` implementation.
4. Several catch proofs tested assertions rather than corrupted inputs passed through validators.
5. `construction_used_carrier_or_action=false` conflated the absent matter carrier/action functional
   with the separately supplied diagonal circle action.
6. Seventeen-node motif agreement is sampled continuation, not a continuous projector-bundle
   theorem. No continuity threshold was preregistered.
7. The production builder's direct amplitude-family and invariant-subspace sources were only
   transitively pinned and must also be named explicitly in this package's lineage table.

## Correction tests

The correction implementation must:

1. independently transform metric/phi two-jets at the 64 frozen blind identities under both stored
   nonlinear coordinate transformations;
2. compare every all-family projector set at every registered path node with the tensor-predicted
   transformed set, retaining numerical uncertainty rather than forcing agreement;
3. report the maximum projector covariance residual and classification discordance count;
4. keep all Frobenius counts explicitly `REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY`; any transformed obstruction probe
   is diagnostic and cannot promote the full census to chart-independent certification;
5. derive Christoffels, the mixed phi Hessian, the gradient dyad, angular gap, and diagonal-generator
   metric-dual connection from the symbolic toric metric rather than from saved eigentuples;
6. directly execute the frozen `hopf_seed` function on a deterministic CPU tensor sample and compare
   it with the metric quotient after inverse stereographic reconstruction;
7. replace ambiguous construction provenance with separate fields for supplied circle action,
   imported `S2` matter carrier, and imported `L2+L4` action functional;
8. exercise mutation tests by passing corrupted in-memory records through the same validators used
   for the unmodified records; direct unconditional throws and tautological length comparisons do not
   count as catches;
9. use sampled-path language everywhere. Large adjacent component distances remain disclosed and no
   smooth bundle, global continuation, or holonomy claim is allowed;
10. add the direct amplitude-family and invariant-subspace manifests to `SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv` and
    verify their manifest contents.

## Fixed thresholds and coverage

- Covariance anchors: the same 64 SHA-256-selected identities used by the frozen independent replay.
- Transforms: both stored nonlinear transformations from the frozen independent motif verifier.
- Families/nodes: all 31 families at all 17 nodes for each anchor and transform.
- Projector covariance gate: maximum relative set distance `<=1e-8` on numerically classified,
  classification-agreeing cases; every uncertain/discordant case retained and counted.
- Direct seed comparison: deterministic 1,000-point float64 CPU sample, maximum absolute residual
  `<=1e-12`.
- Symbolic equalities must simplify exactly to zero.

## Maximum corrected conclusion

At most the conjunction:

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_REGISTERED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS`

and

`EXACT_CONDITIONAL_RECIPROCAL-TORIC/HOPF-SEED_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS`.

Even if every correction test passes, the overall motif-to-Hopf correspondence remains a `LEAD`.
Global continuation, toric-stratum selection, circle action, orientation, caps, deformable carrier
space, action, relaxed field, dynamics, stability, source, mass, and matter emergence remain open.

# Verdict: FAIL

The corrected scientific maximum and `LEAD` status survive, but the package’s `VERIFIED-WITH-CAVEATS` certification does not. The failure concerns the correction contract and verifier strength, not the raw census or toric/Hopf algebra.

## Blocking findings

1. The nonlinear edge-covariance correction is not implemented as claimed.

[verify_review_corrections.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_review_corrections.py:141) reuses the same Jacobian `j` at every path node. The frozen transforms have nonzero second and third jets but constant stored Jacobians ([verify_motif_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_instrument_motif_atlas_2026-07-21/verify_motif_atlas.py:425)). Consequently, the edge test uses a fixed component-frame transformation, not a nonlinear chart whose Jacobian varies along the path.

A post-review read-only probe interpreted those coefficients as global polynomial maps with node-dependent Jacobians. It still found zero discordances over all 63,438 eligible comparisons, so I found no numerical counterexample. However, that post-outcome probe was neither the preregistered implementation nor package evidence and cannot repair the certification retrospectively.

2. Uncertain and skipped covariance cases are not retained and counted as preregistered.

The contract explicitly requires “every uncertain/discordant case retained and counted” ([correction preregistration](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/ADVERSARIAL_REVIEW_CORRECTION_PREREGISTRATION.md:58)). Independent replay found:

- 60 uncertainty-bearing point comparisons: 34 one-sided classified/uncertain and 26 both uncertain.
- 50 of 63,488 possible edge comparisons skipped by the unconditional `continue` at [verify_review_corrections.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_review_corrections.py:198).

None is counted or classified in `REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json`. The report states only 63,438 successful comparisons and zero discordance ([AUDIT_REPORT.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md:84)).

3. The “13 mutation catches” are literal but do not make the validator fail-closed.

All 13 listed mutations are passed through `validate_result` and rejected. But independent mutations of the following load-bearing fields all survived that same validator:

- edge comparison count set to zero;
- intrinsic covariance residual set to `1e9`;
- sampled-path status promoted to `CONTINUOUS_BUNDLE_THEOREM`;
- symbolic angular gap replaced with nonsense;
- seed source SHA-256 corrupted;
- seed sample count reduced from 1,000 to one.

The top-level verifier checks only selected status/count fields ([verify_package.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_package.py:65)). Therefore the 13 catches cannot support the package’s broad correction-validation claim.

# Second-review correction preregistration

Date: 2026-07-22

The second fresh review returned `FAIL` for package certification while explicitly retaining the
scientific maximum and overall `LEAD` status. Its raw return and complete transcript are preserved.
This correction is verification engineering, not a new scientific search, and cannot strengthen the
maximum conclusion.

## Accepted blockers

1. The edge-assignment test reused one Jacobian along a path. Nonzero stored second/third map jets
   made the pointwise geometry test nonlinear, but the edge test was only a fixed component-frame
   transformation.
2. Sixty uncertainty-bearing point comparisons and 50 ineligible transition-edge comparisons were
   omitted from the correction result instead of retained and counted.
3. Six independently corrupted load-bearing result fields survived `validate_result`: edge count,
   intrinsic covariance residual, sampled-path status, symbolic angular gap, seed source hash, and
   seed sample count.

## Registered repair

For each stored `(J,K,L)` transform, define the zero-constant cubic polynomial coordinate map

```text
x(y) = J y + (1/2) K[y,y] + (1/6) L[y,y,y].
```

At every path node, solve `x(y)=x_node`, evaluate the node-dependent Jacobian and second derivative,
and transform the complete metric/phi two-jet. Record maximum inverse-map residual and minimum
absolute Jacobian determinant. This is a newly explicit global-polynomial interpretation of the
stored jets, not a claim that the frozen parent selected a physical chart.

The result must contain:

- all `64*17*31*2 = 67,456` point comparisons;
- a mutually exclusive point-status census: both classified, one-sided uncertain, both uncertain;
- every non-uncertain classification discordance;
- all `64*16*31*2 = 63,488` possible edge comparisons split into tested and skipped;
- every skipped-edge reason and zero silent `continue` accounting;
- every tested-edge transport discordance;
- pointwise tensor/projector residuals under the node-dependent maps.

The validator must enforce all preceding coverage identities and thresholds. It must also enforce:

- intrinsic-object and projector residuals `<=1e-8`;
- exact sampled-path nonpromotion text;
- exact metric-derived angular-gap, connection, and unit-limit records;
- frozen `hopf_seed` source SHA-256, CPU float64 execution, deterministic seed, exactly 1,000
  samples, and residual `<=1e-12`;
- complete construction provenance and direct source lineage; and
- the unchanged maximum and overall `LEAD` status.

Mutation catches must include the six escaped mutations, missing uncertainty counts, missing skipped
edges, and replacement of the node-dependent polynomial-map interpretation with a fixed Jacobian.

## Known review probe

The second reviewer independently applied this cubic-polynomial interpretation after finding the
defect and observed zero discordances on the eligible edges. That post-review outcome is known and
cannot be presented as outcome-blind. The package implementation must nevertheless recompute it from
scratch, retain every excluded/uncertain case, and survive another fresh audit before certification.

## Maximum conclusion

Unchanged:

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_REGISTERED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS`

plus

`EXACT_CONDITIONAL_RECIPROCAL-TORIC/HOPF-SEED_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS`.

The proposed motif-to-Hopf correspondence remains a `LEAD`. No continuous/global continuation,
physical chart, toric/circle selection, cap, carrier, action, dynamics, stability, source, or mass is
derived.

===== udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/CORRECTED_FRESH_REVIEW_RAW.md =====
# Verdict: FAIL

The corrected scientific maximum and `LEAD` status survive, but the package’s `VERIFIED-WITH-CAVEATS` certification does not. The failure concerns the correction contract and verifier strength, not the raw census or toric/Hopf algebra.

## Blocking findings

1. The nonlinear edge-covariance correction is not implemented as claimed.

[verify_review_corrections.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_review_corrections.py:141) reuses the same Jacobian `j` at every path node. The frozen transforms have nonzero second and third jets but constant stored Jacobians ([verify_motif_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_instrument_motif_atlas_2026-07-21/verify_motif_atlas.py:425)). Consequently, the edge test uses a fixed component-frame transformation, not a nonlinear chart whose Jacobian varies along the path.

A post-review read-only probe interpreted those coefficients as global polynomial maps with node-dependent Jacobians. It still found zero discordances over all 63,438 eligible comparisons, so I found no numerical counterexample. However, that post-outcome probe was neither the preregistered implementation nor package evidence and cannot repair the certification retrospectively.

2. Uncertain and skipped covariance cases are not retained and counted as preregistered.

The contract explicitly requires “every uncertain/discordant case retained and counted” ([correction preregistration](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/ADVERSARIAL_REVIEW_CORRECTION_PREREGISTRATION.md:58)). Independent replay found:

- 60 uncertainty-bearing point comparisons: 34 one-sided classified/uncertain and 26 both uncertain.
- 50 of 63,488 possible edge comparisons skipped by the unconditional `continue` at [verify_review_corrections.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_review_corrections.py:198).

None is counted or classified in `REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json`. The report states only 63,438 successful comparisons and zero discordance ([AUDIT_REPORT.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md:84)).

3. The “13 mutation catches” are literal but do not make the validator fail-closed.

All 13 listed mutations are passed through `validate_result` and rejected. But independent mutations of the following load-bearing fields all survived that same validator:

- edge comparison count set to zero;
- intrinsic covariance residual set to `1e9`;
- sampled-path status promoted to `CONTINUOUS_BUNDLE_THEOREM`;
- symbolic angular gap replaced with nonsense;
- seed source SHA-256 corrupted;
- seed sample count reduced from 1,000 to one.

The top-level verifier checks only selected status/count fields ([verify_package.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_package.py:65)). Therefore the 13 catches cannot support the package’s broad correction-validation claim.

## Findings that passed

- An unchanged temporary-copy execution of `verify_package.py` reproduced all three banked outputs byte-for-byte.
- Raw-ledger keys are unique and counts reproduce exactly: 3,072 identities, 1,618,944 path rows, 95,232 summaries, and 143,487 distribution rows.
- All distribution records retain `GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT`; all 13 uncertain stencils remain present.
- Frobenius claims are honestly restricted to `REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY`.
- Independent metric algebra reproduced
  \[
  H^\mu{}_\nu=\mathrm{diag}\left(0,-A'/A^3,\frac{\Omega'/\Omega-1}{A^2},\frac{\Omega'/\Omega+1}{A^2}\right),
  \]
  angular gap \(2/A^2\), and
  \[
  \mathcal A=\frac{d\xi_1+e^{4\phi}d\xi_2}{1+e^{4\phi}}.
  \]
- Independent direct execution of the frozen `hopf_seed` agreed at maximum residual \(6.46\times10^{-15}\).
- Frozen-source hashes and manifest contents passed.
- The supplied circle action, absent construction-time `S2` carrier, and absent `L2+L4` functional are correctly separated in the report.
- Sampled-path wording and overall `LEAD` status are appropriately conservative.

## Four evidence gates

1. Preregistered: **NO** for the correction as executed; uncertainty accounting and genuine path-dependent nonlinear coordinates were not implemented.
2. Full space or bounded scope: **YES** for the registered raw census; incomplete for the claimed covariance accounting.
3. Independently verified: **YES** for the bounded census and toric/seed witness; **NO** for the package’s fail-closed covariance certification.
4. Premises audited: **YES in the scientific prose**, but incompletely enforced by machine validators.

## Strongest honest maximum

The evidence still supports, but does not package-certify as fully corrected:

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_REGISTERED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS`

plus

`EXACT_CONDITIONAL_RECIPROCAL-TORIC/HOPF-SEED_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS`.

The overall motif-to-Hopf correspondence remains a `LEAD`. Continuous/global continuation, toric-stratum and circle-action selection, caps, carrier emergence, action, dynamics, stability, source, and mass remain open.

No repository file was intentionally edited; all write-producing verification ran in a temporary mirror.

===== udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/SECOND_REVIEW_CORRECTION_PREREGISTRATION.md =====
# Second-review correction preregistration

Date: 2026-07-22

The second fresh review returned `FAIL` for package certification while explicitly retaining the
scientific maximum and overall `LEAD` status. Its raw return and complete transcript are preserved.
This correction is verification engineering, not a new scientific search, and cannot strengthen the
maximum conclusion.

## Accepted blockers

1. The edge-assignment test reused one Jacobian along a path. Nonzero stored second/third map jets
   made the pointwise geometry test nonlinear, but the edge test was only a fixed component-frame
   transformation.
2. Sixty uncertainty-bearing point comparisons and 50 ineligible transition-edge comparisons were
   omitted from the correction result instead of retained and counted.
3. Six independently corrupted load-bearing result fields survived `validate_result`: edge count,
   intrinsic covariance residual, sampled-path status, symbolic angular gap, seed source hash, and
   seed sample count.

## Registered repair

For each stored `(J,K,L)` transform, define the zero-constant cubic polynomial coordinate map

```text
x(y) = J y + (1/2) K[y,y] + (1/6) L[y,y,y].
```

At every path node, solve `x(y)=x_node`, evaluate the node-dependent Jacobian and second derivative,
and transform the complete metric/phi two-jet. Record maximum inverse-map residual and minimum
absolute Jacobian determinant. This is a newly explicit global-polynomial interpretation of the
stored jets, not a claim that the frozen parent selected a physical chart.

The result must contain:

- all `64*17*31*2 = 67,456` point comparisons;
- a mutually exclusive point-status census: both classified, one-sided uncertain, both uncertain;
- every non-uncertain classification discordance;
- all `64*16*31*2 = 63,488` possible edge comparisons split into tested and skipped;
- every skipped-edge reason and zero silent `continue` accounting;
- every tested-edge transport discordance;
- pointwise tensor/projector residuals under the node-dependent maps.

The validator must enforce all preceding coverage identities and thresholds. It must also enforce:

- intrinsic-object and projector residuals `<=1e-8`;
- exact sampled-path nonpromotion text;
- exact metric-derived angular-gap, connection, and unit-limit records;
- frozen `hopf_seed` source SHA-256, CPU float64 execution, deterministic seed, exactly 1,000
  samples, and residual `<=1e-12`;
- complete construction provenance and direct source lineage; and
- the unchanged maximum and overall `LEAD` status.

Mutation catches must include the six escaped mutations, missing uncertainty counts, missing skipped
edges, and replacement of the node-dependent polynomial-map interpretation with a fixed Jacobian.

## Known review probe

The second reviewer independently applied this cubic-polynomial interpretation after finding the
defect and observed zero discordances on the eligible edges. That post-review outcome is known and
cannot be presented as outcome-blind. The package implementation must nevertheless recompute it from
scratch, retain every excluded/uncertain case, and survive another fresh audit before certification.

## Maximum conclusion

Unchanged:

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_REGISTERED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS`

plus

`EXACT_CONDITIONAL_RECIPROCAL-TORIC/HOPF-SEED_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS`.

The proposed motif-to-Hopf correspondence remains a `LEAD`. No continuous/global continuation,
physical chart, toric/circle selection, cap, carrier, action, dynamics, stability, source, or mass is
derived.

===== udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/CORRECTION_VERIFIER_IMPLEMENTATION_NOTE.md =====
# Correction-verifier implementation note

Date: 2026-07-22

The first execution of `verify_review_corrections.py` exited before writing any result. The symbolic
metric derivation reached its final connection/quotient assertion, where SymPy left

```text
exp(-2*phi)/(2*cosh(2*phi)) - 1/(exp(4*phi)+1)
```

unsimplified. Rewriting that expression in exponentials reduces it exactly to zero. The quotient
norm and full-range limit already reduced to `0` and `1` respectively.

Before changing the verifier, the registered implementation correction is: apply `.rewrite(exp)`
before simplifying the connection residual. No threshold, sample, metric, target formula, or result
classification changes. The full covariance computation will be rerun rather than recovered from
memory.

    64	def digest(path: Path) -> str:
    65	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    66	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    67	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):
    68	            value.update(block)
    69	    return value.hexdigest()

    72	def read_tsv(path: Path) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
    73	    with path.open(encoding="utf-8", newline="") as handle:
    74	        return list(csv.DictReader(handle, delimiter="\t"))

    77	def family_results(objects: dict[str, object], metric: np.ndarray) -> dict[int, dict[str, object]]:
    78	    scalar = {key: objects[key] for key in ("R", "H", "D")}
    79	    return {
    80	        mask: reconstructed.independent.classify(
    81	            reconstructed.independent.operators(objects, keys),
    82	            objects["gradient"], metric, scalar, keys,
    83	        )
    84	        for _family_id, mask, keys in reconstructed.FAMILIES
    85	    }

    87	
    88	def labels(result: dict[str, object]) -> list[tuple[int, str]]:
    89	    return [(int(item["rank"]), str(item["signature"])) for item in result["blocks"]]
    90	
    91	
    92	def assignment(
    93	    first: dict[str, object],
    94	    second: dict[str, object],
    95	    first_projectors: list[np.ndarray] | None = None,
    96	    second_projectors: list[np.ndarray] | None = None,
    97	) -> tuple[int, ...] | None:
    98	    first_labels = labels(first)
    99	    second_labels = labels(second)
   100	    if Counter(first_labels) != Counter(second_labels):
   101	        return None
   102	    left = first_projectors or [np.asarray(item) for item in first["projectors"]]
   103	    right = second_projectors or [np.asarray(item) for item in second["projectors"]]
   104	    best: tuple[int, ...] | None = None
   105	    best_distance = math.inf
   106	    for permutation in itertools.permutations(range(len(right))):
   107	        if any(first_labels[index] != second_labels[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(left))):
   108	            continue
   109	        distance = max(
   110	            (reconstructed.independent.relmax(left[index], right[permutation[index]])
   111	             for index in range(len(left))),
   112	            default=0.0,
   113	        )
   114	        if distance < best_distance:
   115	            best = tuple(permutation)
   116	            best_distance = distance
   117	    return best
   118	
   119	
   120	def polynomial_map_value(
   121	    jacobian: np.ndarray,
   122	    jacobian_first: np.ndarray,
   123	    jacobian_second: np.ndarray,
   124	    point: np.ndarray,
   125	) -> np.ndarray:
   126	    return (
   127	        jacobian @ point
   128	        + 0.5 * np.einsum("mab,a,b->m", jacobian_first, point, point)
   129	        + (1.0 / 6.0) * np.einsum("mabc,a,b,c->m", jacobian_second, point, point, point)
   130	    )
   131	
   132	
   133	def polynomial_map_local_jets(
   134	    jacobian: np.ndarray,
   135	    jacobian_first: np.ndarray,
   136	    jacobian_second: np.ndarray,
   137	    point: np.ndarray,
   138	) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
   139	    local_jacobian = (
   140	        jacobian
   141	        + np.einsum("mab,b->ma", jacobian_first, point)
   142	        + 0.5 * np.einsum("mabc,b,c->ma", jacobian_second, point, point)
   143	    )
   144	    local_first = jacobian_first + np.einsum("mabc,c->mab", jacobian_second, point)
   145	    return local_jacobian, local_first, jacobian_second
   146	
   147	
   148	def invert_polynomial_map(
   149	    jacobian: np.ndarray,
   150	    jacobian_first: np.ndarray,
   151	    jacobian_second: np.ndarray,
   152	    target: np.ndarray,
   153	) -> tuple[np.ndarray, float]:
   154	    point = np.linalg.solve(jacobian, target)
   155	    for _iteration in range(30):
   156	        local_jacobian, _local_first, _local_second = polynomial_map_local_jets(
   157	            jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second, point
   158	        )
   159	        residual = polynomial_map_value(
   160	            jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second, point
   161	        ) - target
   162	        step = np.linalg.solve(local_jacobian, residual)
   163	        point -= step
   164	        if float(np.max(np.abs(step))) < 1.0e-14:
   165	            break
   166	    residual = float(np.max(np.abs(
   167	        polynomial_map_value(jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second, point) - target
   168	    )))
   169	    if residual > 1.0e-11:
   170	        raise AssertionError(f"polynomial map inversion {residual}")
   171	    return point, residual
   172	
   173	
   174	def covariance_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   175	    lookup = reconstructed.identity_data()
   176	    identities = sorted(
   177	        lookup,
   178	        key=lambda value: hashlib.sha256(
   179	            ("MOTIF_HOPF_INDEPENDENT_V1|" + value).encode()
   180	        ).hexdigest(),
   181	    )[:64]
   182	    transforms = reconstructed.independent.transforms()
   183	    comparisons = 0
   184	    nonuncertain_discordances = 0
   185	    maximum_object_residual = 0.0
   186	    maximum_projector_residual = 0.0
   187	    maximum_inverse_map_residual = 0.0
   188	    minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant = math.inf
   189	    point_status_census: Counter[str] = Counter()
   190	    edge_comparisons = 0
   191	    edge_discordances = 0
   192	    edge_total = 0
   193	    edge_skips: Counter[str] = Counter()
   194	
   195	    for identity_id in identities:
   196	        bank, amplitudes = lookup[identity_id]
   197	        original_nodes: list[dict[int, dict[str, object]]] = []
   198	        transformed_nodes: dict[str, list[dict[int, dict[str, object]]]] = {
   199	            transform_id: [] for transform_id, *_rest in transforms
   200	        }
   201	        point_maps: dict[str, list[dict[int, tuple[int, ...] | None]]] = {
   202	            transform_id: [] for transform_id, *_rest in transforms
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        for point in reconstructed.path_points(bank):
   206	            g, dg, ddg, phi_first, phi_second = reconstructed.metric_phi_jets(
   207	                bank, amplitudes, point
   208	            )
   209	            objects, _geometry = reconstructed.independent.objects(
   210	                g, dg, ddg, phi_first, phi_second
   211	            )
   212	            originals = family_results(objects, g)
   213	            original_nodes.append(originals)
   214	
   215	            for transform_id, registered_jacobian, registered_first, registered_second in transforms:
   216	                mapped_point, inverse_residual = invert_polynomial_map(
   217	                    registered_jacobian, registered_first, registered_second, point
   218	                )
   219	                jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second = polynomial_map_local_jets(
   220	                    registered_jacobian, registered_first, registered_second, mapped_point
   221	                )
   222	                determinant = abs(float(np.linalg.det(jacobian)))
   223	                minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant = min(
   224	                    minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant, determinant
   225	                )
   226	                maximum_inverse_map_residual = max(
   227	                    maximum_inverse_map_residual, inverse_residual
   228	                )
   229	                transformed = reconstructed.independent.transform_jets(
   230	                    g, dg, ddg, 0.0, phi_first, phi_second,
   231	                    jacobian, jacobian_first, jacobian_second,
   232	                )
   233	                transformed_objects, _transformed_geometry = reconstructed.independent.objects(
   234	                    transformed[0], transformed[1], transformed[2],
   235	                    transformed[4], transformed[5],
   236	                )
   237	                transformed_results = family_results(transformed_objects, transformed[0])
   238	                transformed_nodes[transform_id].append(transformed_results)
   239	                inverse = np.linalg.inv(jacobian)
   240	                maximum_object_residual = max(
   241	                    maximum_object_residual,
   242	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["metric"], jacobian.T @ g @ jacobian),
   243	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["gradient"], inverse @ objects["gradient"]),
   244	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["R"], inverse @ objects["R"] @ jacobian),
   245	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["H"], inverse @ objects["H"] @ jacobian),
   246	                    reconstructed.independent.relmax(transformed_objects["D"], inverse @ objects["D"] @ jacobian),
   247	                )
   248	                current_maps: dict[int, tuple[int, ...] | None] = {}
   249	                for _family_id, mask, _keys in reconstructed.FAMILIES:
   250	                    original = originals[mask]
   251	                    current = transformed_results[mask]
   252	                    comparisons += 1
   253	                    discordant = [field for field in COMPARE if original[field] != current[field]]
   254	                    both_classified = (
   255	                        original["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   256	                        and current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   257	                    )
   258	                    if both_classified:
   259	                        point_status_census["BOTH_CLASSIFIED"] += 1
   260	                    elif (
   261	                        original["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   262	                    ) != (
   263	                        current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED"
   264	                    ):
   265	                        point_status_census["ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN"] += 1
   266	                    else:
   267	                        point_status_census["BOTH_UNCERTAIN"] += 1
   268	                    if both_classified and discordant:
   269	                        nonuncertain_discordances += 1
   270	                    predicted = [inverse @ np.asarray(item) @ jacobian for item in original["projectors"]]
   271	                    if both_classified and not discordant:
   272	                        residual = reconstructed.independent.set_distance(
   273	                            predicted,
   274	                            [np.asarray(item) for item in current["projectors"]],
   275	                        )
   276	                        maximum_projector_residual = max(maximum_projector_residual, residual)
   277	                    current_maps[mask] = assignment(original, current, predicted)
   278	                point_maps[transform_id].append(current_maps)
   279	
   280	        # Compare the actual minimum-distance edge assignment with the assignment predicted by
   281	        # pointwise tensor covariance. This is the preregistered path-matching covariance gate.
   282	        for transform_id, *_rest in transforms:
   283	            current_nodes = transformed_nodes[transform_id]
   284	            maps = point_maps[transform_id]
   285	            for node in range(16):
   286	                for _family_id, mask, _keys in reconstructed.FAMILIES:
   287	                    left = original_nodes[node][mask]
   288	                    right = original_nodes[node + 1][mask]
   289	                    transformed_left = current_nodes[node][mask]
   290	                    transformed_right = current_nodes[node + 1][mask]
   291	                    original_edge = assignment(left, right)
   292	                    transformed_edge = assignment(transformed_left, transformed_right)
   293	                    left_map = maps[node][mask]
   294	                    right_map = maps[node + 1][mask]
   295	                    edge_total += 1
   296	                    if None in (original_edge, transformed_edge, left_map, right_map):
   297	                        reasons = []
   298	                        if original_edge is None:
   299	                            reasons.append("ORIGINAL_EDGE_UNMATCHED")
   300	                        if transformed_edge is None:
   301	                            reasons.append("TRANSFORMED_EDGE_UNMATCHED")
   302	                        if left_map is None:
   303	                            reasons.append("LEFT_POINT_COVARIANCE_MAP_UNMATCHED")
   304	                        if right_map is None:
   305	                            reasons.append("RIGHT_POINT_COVARIANCE_MAP_UNMATCHED")
   306	                        edge_skips["+".join(reasons)] += 1
   307	                        continue
   308	                    predicted = [None] * len(left_map)
   309	                    for original_left, transformed_left_index in enumerate(left_map):
   310	                        original_right = original_edge[original_left]
   311	                        predicted[transformed_left_index] = right_map[original_right]
   312	                    edge_comparisons += 1
   313	                    if tuple(predicted) != transformed_edge:
   314	                        edge_discordances += 1
   315	
   316	    return {
   317	        "coordinate_map_interpretation": MAP_INTERPRETATION,
   318	        "coordinate_map_evidence_status": "CONFIRMATORY_POST_SECOND_REVIEW_REPAIR",
   319	        "blind_identities": len(identities),
   320	        "stored_nonlinear_transforms": len(transforms),
   321	        "all_family_node_comparisons": comparisons,
   322	        "nonuncertain_classification_discordances": nonuncertain_discordances,
   323	        "maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual": maximum_object_residual,
   324	        "maximum_projector_set_covariance_residual": maximum_projector_residual,
   325	        "maximum_inverse_map_residual": maximum_inverse_map_residual,
   326	        "minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant": minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant,
   327	        "point_status_census": dict(sorted(point_status_census.items())),
   328	        "uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons": (
   329	            point_status_census["ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN"]
   330	            + point_status_census["BOTH_UNCERTAIN"]
   331	        ),
   332	        "possible_edge_transport_comparisons": edge_total,
   333	        "matched_edge_transport_comparisons": edge_comparisons,
   334	        "skipped_edge_transport_comparisons": sum(edge_skips.values()),
   335	        "skipped_edge_reason_census": dict(sorted(edge_skips.items())),
   336	        "matched_edge_transport_discordances": edge_discordances,
   337	    }

   340	def symbolic_toric_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   341	    time, phi, xi1, xi2 = sp.symbols("t phi xi1 xi2", real=True)
   342	    coordinates = (time, phi, xi1, xi2)
   343	    radial = sp.Function("A", positive=True)(phi)
   344	    common = sp.Function("Omega", positive=True)(phi)
   345	    metric = sp.diag(
   346	        -1,
   347	        radial**2,
   348	        common**2 * sp.exp(-2 * phi),
   349	        common**2 * sp.exp(2 * phi),
   350	    )
   351	    inverse = sp.simplify(metric.inv())
   352	    gamma = [[[
   353	        sp.simplify(sum(
   354	            inverse[upper, lower] * (
   355	                sp.diff(metric[lower, right], coordinates[left])
   356	                + sp.diff(metric[lower, left], coordinates[right])
   357	                - sp.diff(metric[left, right], coordinates[lower])
   358	            )
   359	            for lower in range(4)
   360	        ) / 2)

   340	def symbolic_toric_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   341	    time, phi, xi1, xi2 = sp.symbols("t phi xi1 xi2", real=True)
   342	    coordinates = (time, phi, xi1, xi2)
   343	    radial = sp.Function("A", positive=True)(phi)
   344	    common = sp.Function("Omega", positive=True)(phi)
   345	    metric = sp.diag(
   346	        -1,
   347	        radial**2,
   348	        common**2 * sp.exp(-2 * phi),
   349	        common**2 * sp.exp(2 * phi),
   350	    )
   351	    inverse = sp.simplify(metric.inv())
   352	    gamma = [[[
   353	        sp.simplify(sum(
   354	            inverse[upper, lower] * (
   355	                sp.diff(metric[lower, right], coordinates[left])
   356	                + sp.diff(metric[lower, left], coordinates[right])
   357	                - sp.diff(metric[left, right], coordinates[lower])
   358	            )
   359	            for lower in range(4)
   360	        ) / 2)
   361	        for right in range(4)] for left in range(4)] for upper in range(4)]
   362	    hessian = sp.Matrix(
   363	        4, 4,
   364	        lambda upper, lower: sp.simplify(
   365	            -sum(inverse[upper, index] * gamma[1][index][lower] for index in range(4))
   366	        ),
   367	    )
   368	    dyad = sp.zeros(4)
   369	    dyad[1, 1] = inverse[1, 1]
   370	    expected_hessian = sp.diag(
   371	        0,
   372	        -sp.diff(radial, phi) / radial**3,
   373	        (sp.diff(common, phi) / common - 1) / radial**2,
   374	        (sp.diff(common, phi) / common + 1) / radial**2,
   375	    )
   376	    expected_dyad = sp.diag(0, radial**-2, 0, 0)
   377	    hessian_residual = sp.simplify(hessian - expected_hessian)
   378	    dyad_residual = sp.simplify(dyad - expected_dyad)
   379	    angular_gap = sp.simplify(hessian[3, 3] - hessian[2, 2])
   380	
   381	    diagonal_generator = sp.Matrix((0, 0, 1, 1))
   382	    generator_flat = metric * diagonal_generator
   383	    generator_norm = sp.simplify((diagonal_generator.T * metric * diagonal_generator)[0])
   384	    connection = [sp.simplify(value / generator_norm) for value in generator_flat]
   385	    weight = sp.simplify(connection[2])
   386	    expected_weight = sp.simplify(1 / (1 + sp.exp(4 * phi)))
   387	    connection_residual = sp.simplify((weight - expected_weight).rewrite(sp.exp))
   388	    quotient = sp.Matrix((
   389	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.cos(xi1 - xi2),
   390	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.sin(xi1 - xi2),
   391	        -sp.tanh(2 * phi),
   392	    ))
   393	    quotient_norm_residual = sp.simplify((quotient.dot(quotient) - 1).rewrite(sp.exp))
   394	    unit_limit = sp.simplify(
   395	        sp.limit(weight, phi, -sp.oo) - sp.limit(weight, phi, sp.oo)
   396	    )
   397	    if hessian_residual != sp.zeros(4) or dyad_residual != sp.zeros(4):
   398	        raise AssertionError("symbolic metric derivation")
   399	    if sp.simplify(angular_gap - 2 / radial**2) != 0:
   400	        raise AssertionError("symbolic angular gap")
   401	    if connection_residual != 0 or quotient_norm_residual != 0 or unit_limit != 1:
   402	        raise AssertionError("symbolic connection/quotient")
   403	    return {
   404	        "christoffels_derived_from_metric": True,
   405	        "mixed_hessian_derived_from_metric": True,
   406	        "gradient_dyad_derived_from_metric": True,
   407	        "angular_gap": str(angular_gap),
   408	        "diagonal_connection_weight": str(weight),
   409	        "connection_common_scale_cancelled": not weight.has(common),
   410	        "quotient_norm_exact": quotient_norm_residual == 0,
   411	        "conditional_full_range_unit_limit": str(unit_limit),
   412	    }

   415	def direct_hopf_seed_audit() -> dict[str, object]:
   416	    source = ROOT / "hopfion_arc_scripts_2026-07-05/fs_hopfion.py"
   417	    tree = ast.parse(source.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   418	    if not any(isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef) and node.name == "hopf_seed" for node in tree.body):
   419	        raise AssertionError("hopf_seed function absent")
   420	    specification = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("frozen_hopf_seed_module", source)
   421	    if specification is None or specification.loader is None:
   422	        raise AssertionError("hopf_seed import specification")
   423	    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(specification)
   424	    specification.loader.exec_module(module)
   425	    import torch
   426	
   427	    if module.dev != "cpu":
   428	        raise AssertionError("CPU-only seed replay")
   429	    generator = np.random.default_rng(20260722)
   430	    phi = generator.uniform(-2.0, 2.0, 1000)
   431	    xi1 = generator.uniform(-math.pi, math.pi, 1000)
   432	    xi2 = generator.uniform(-math.pi, math.pi, 1000)
   433	    eta = np.arctan(np.exp(2 * phi))
   434	    s1 = np.cos(eta) * np.cos(xi1)
   435	    s2 = np.cos(eta) * np.sin(xi1)
   436	    s3 = np.sin(eta) * np.cos(xi2)
   437	    s4 = np.sin(eta) * np.sin(xi2)
   438	    scale = 1.7
   439	    denominator = 1 + s4
   440	    x = scale * s1 / denominator
   441	    y = scale * s2 / denominator
   442	    z = scale * s3 / denominator
   443	    with torch.no_grad():
   444	        actual = module.hopf_seed(
   445	            torch.as_tensor(x, dtype=torch.float64),
   446	            torch.as_tensor(y, dtype=torch.float64),
   447	            torch.as_tensor(z, dtype=torch.float64),
   448	            scale,
   449	        ).cpu().numpy()
   450	    delta = xi1 - xi2
   451	    expected = np.asarray((
   452	        np.cosh(2 * phi) ** -1 * np.cos(delta),
   453	        np.cosh(2 * phi) ** -1 * np.sin(delta),
   454	        -np.tanh(2 * phi),
   455	    ))
   456	    residual = float(np.max(np.abs(actual - expected)))
   457	    return {
   458	        "source_path": str(source.relative_to(ROOT)),
   459	        "source_sha256": digest(source),
   460	        "function_executed": "hopf_seed",
   461	        "device": module.dev,
   462	        "dtype": "float64",
   463	        "sample_points": 1000,
   464	        "sample_seed": 20260722,
   465	        "maximum_absolute_residual": residual,
   466	    }

   469	def validate_source_lineage(rows: list[dict[str, str]]) -> None:
   470	    if len(rows) != 10 or len({row["path"] for row in rows}) != 10:
   471	        raise AssertionError("complete source lineage")
   472	    indexed = {row["path"]: row["sha256"] for row in rows}
   473	    for relative, expected in DIRECT_SOURCES.items():
   474	        if indexed.get(relative) != expected:
   475	            raise AssertionError(f"direct source lineage {relative}")
   476	        if digest(ROOT / relative) != expected:
   477	            raise AssertionError(f"direct source manifest identity {relative}")
   478	        package = ROOT / Path(relative).parent
   479	        for line in (package / "SHA256SUMS.txt").read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
   480	            if not line.strip():
   481	                continue
   482	            wanted, name = line.split(maxsplit=1)
   483	            if digest(package / name.strip()) != wanted:
   484	                raise AssertionError(f"direct source manifest content {relative}:{name}")
   485	
   486	
   487	def validate_result(result: dict[str, object], lineage: list[dict[str, str]]) -> None:
   488	    covariance = result["covariance"]
   489	    symbolic = result["symbolic_toric"]
   490	    seed = result["direct_hopf_seed"]
   491	    provenance = result["construction_provenance"]
   492	    if covariance["blind_identities"] != 64 or covariance["stored_nonlinear_transforms"] != 2:
   493	        raise AssertionError("covariance anchor coverage")
   494	    if covariance["all_family_node_comparisons"] != 64 * 17 * 31 * 2:
   495	        raise AssertionError("covariance family/node coverage")
   496	    point_status = covariance["point_status_census"]
   497	    if point_status != EXPECTED_POINT_STATUS:
   498	        raise AssertionError("exact point status census")
   499	    if any(not isinstance(value, int) or value < 0 for value in point_status.values()):
   500	        raise AssertionError("nonnegative integer point status counts")
   501	    if sum(point_status.values()) != covariance["all_family_node_comparisons"]:
   502	        raise AssertionError("point status completeness")
   503	    if covariance["uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons"] != (
   504	        point_status["ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN"] + point_status["BOTH_UNCERTAIN"]
   505	    ):
   506	        raise AssertionError("uncertainty accounting")
   507	    if covariance["nonuncertain_classification_discordances"] != 0:
   508	        raise AssertionError("coordinate classification discordance")
   509	    if covariance["coordinate_map_interpretation"] != MAP_INTERPRETATION:
   510	        raise AssertionError("node-dependent nonlinear coordinate map")
   511	    if covariance["coordinate_map_evidence_status"] != "CONFIRMATORY_POST_SECOND_REVIEW_REPAIR":
   512	        raise AssertionError("coordinate map evidence provenance")
   513	    if not math.isfinite(covariance["maximum_inverse_map_residual"]) or not (
   514	        0 <= covariance["maximum_inverse_map_residual"] <= 1.0e-11
   515	    ):
   516	        raise AssertionError("coordinate map inverse residual")
   517	    if not math.isfinite(covariance["minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant"]) or (
   518	        covariance["minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant"] <= 1.0e-6
   519	    ):
   520	        raise AssertionError("coordinate map Jacobian degeneracy")
   521	    if not math.isfinite(covariance["maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual"]) or not (
   522	        0 <= covariance["maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual"] <= COVARIANCE_TOLERANCE
   523	    ):
   524	        raise AssertionError("intrinsic object covariance residual")
   525	    if not math.isfinite(covariance["maximum_projector_set_covariance_residual"]) or not (
   526	        0 <= covariance["maximum_projector_set_covariance_residual"] <= COVARIANCE_TOLERANCE
   527	    ):
   528	        raise AssertionError("projector covariance residual")
   529	    if covariance["possible_edge_transport_comparisons"] != EXPECTED_POSSIBLE_EDGES:
   530	        raise AssertionError("possible edge coverage")
   531	    if covariance["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"] != EXPECTED_MATCHED_EDGES:
   532	        raise AssertionError("exact matched edge coverage")
   533	    if covariance["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"] != EXPECTED_SKIPPED_EDGES:
   534	        raise AssertionError("exact skipped edge coverage")
   535	    if covariance["skipped_edge_reason_census"] != EXPECTED_SKIP_REASONS:
   536	        raise AssertionError("exact skipped edge reason census")
   537	    if covariance["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"] + covariance["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"] != covariance["possible_edge_transport_comparisons"]:
   538	        raise AssertionError("edge comparison accounting")
   539	    if sum(covariance["skipped_edge_reason_census"].values()) != covariance["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"]:
   540	        raise AssertionError("skipped edge reason accounting")
   541	    if covariance["matched_edge_transport_discordances"] != 0:
   542	        raise AssertionError("path matching covariance")
   543	    if result["frobenius_certification_scope"] != "REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY":
   544	        raise AssertionError("Frobenius scope promotion")
   545	    required_symbolic = (
   546	        "christoffels_derived_from_metric", "mixed_hessian_derived_from_metric",
   547	        "gradient_dyad_derived_from_metric", "connection_common_scale_cancelled",
   548	        "quotient_norm_exact",
   549	    )
   550	    if not all(symbolic[key] is True for key in required_symbolic):
   551	        raise AssertionError("symbolic toric derivation")
   552	    if symbolic["angular_gap"] != "2/A(phi)**2":
   553	        raise AssertionError("symbolic angular gap")
   554	    if symbolic["diagonal_connection_weight"] != "exp(-2*phi)/(2*cosh(2*phi))":
   555	        raise AssertionError("symbolic connection weight")
   556	    if symbolic["conditional_full_range_unit_limit"] != "1":
   557	        raise AssertionError("symbolic unit limit")
   558	    if seed["source_path"] != HOPF_SEED_PATH:
   559	        raise AssertionError("direct seed source path")
   560	    if seed["function_executed"] != "hopf_seed" or seed["device"] != "cpu":
   561	        raise AssertionError("direct seed execution")
   562	    if seed["source_sha256"] != HOPF_SEED_SHA256:
   563	        raise AssertionError("direct seed source identity")
   564	    if seed["dtype"] != "float64" or seed["sample_points"] != 1000 or seed["sample_seed"] != 20260722:
   565	        raise AssertionError("direct seed sample contract")
   566	    if not math.isfinite(seed["maximum_absolute_residual"]) or not (
   567	        0 <= seed["maximum_absolute_residual"] <= SEED_TOLERANCE
   568	    ):
   569	        raise AssertionError("direct seed residual")
   570	    if provenance != {
   571	        "supplied_equal_weight_circle_action": True,
   572	        "imported_s2_matter_carrier": False,
   573	        "imported_l2_l4_action_functional": False,
   574	    }:
   575	        raise AssertionError("construction provenance")
   576	    if result["overall_correspondence_status"] != "LEAD":
   577	        raise AssertionError("correspondence promotion")
   578	    if result["sampled_path_status"] != SAMPLED_STATUS:
   579	        raise AssertionError("sampled path promotion")
   580	    if result["maximum_conclusion"] != MAXIMUM:
   581	        raise AssertionError("maximum conclusion")
   582	    validate_source_lineage(lineage)
   583	
   584	
   585	def mutation_catches(
   586	    result: dict[str, object], lineage: list[dict[str, str]]
   587	) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
   588	    mutations = []
   589	
   590	    def add(name: str, mutate) -> None:
   591	        candidate = copy.deepcopy(result)
   592	        candidate_lineage = copy.deepcopy(lineage)
   593	        mutate(candidate, candidate_lineage)
   594	        try:
   595	            validate_result(candidate, candidate_lineage)
   596	        except AssertionError:
   597	            mutations.append({"catch_id": name, "result": "MUTATION_REJECTED"})
   598	            return
   599	        raise AssertionError(f"mutation survived {name}")
   600	
   601	    add("K01_MISSING_COVARIANCE_COMPARISON", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   602	        "all_family_node_comparisons", item["covariance"]["all_family_node_comparisons"] - 1
   603	    ))
   604	    add("K02_DUPLICATE_COVARIANCE_COMPARISON", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   605	        "all_family_node_comparisons", item["covariance"]["all_family_node_comparisons"] + 1
   606	    ))
   607	    add("K03_PROJECTOR_COVARIANCE_FAILURE", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   608	        "maximum_projector_set_covariance_residual", 1.0e-3
   609	    ))
   610	    add("K04_CLASSIFICATION_DISCORDANCE", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   611	        "nonuncertain_classification_discordances", 1
   612	    ))
   613	    add("K05_PATH_MATCHING_DISCORDANCE", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   614	        "matched_edge_transport_discordances", 1
   615	    ))
   616	    add("K06_FROBENIUS_SCOPE_PROMOTION", lambda item, _rows: item.__setitem__(
   617	        "frobenius_certification_scope", "CHART_INDEPENDENT"
   618	    ))
   619	    add("K07_CIRCULAR_TORIC_FORMULA", lambda item, _rows: item["symbolic_toric"].__setitem__(
   620	        "christoffels_derived_from_metric", False
   621	    ))
   622	    add("K08_SEED_BEHAVIOR_MISMATCH", lambda item, _rows: item["direct_hopf_seed"].__setitem__(
   623	        "maximum_absolute_residual", 1.0e-4
   624	    ))
   625	    add("K09_OMITTED_SUPPLIED_CIRCLE_ACTION", lambda item, _rows: item["construction_provenance"].__setitem__(
   626	        "supplied_equal_weight_circle_action", False
   627	    ))
   628	    add("K10_IMPORTED_S2_CARRIER", lambda item, _rows: item["construction_provenance"].__setitem__(
   629	        "imported_s2_matter_carrier", True
   630	    ))
   631	    add("K11_IMPORTED_L2_L4_ACTION", lambda item, _rows: item["construction_provenance"].__setitem__(
   632	        "imported_l2_l4_action_functional", True
   633	    ))
   634	    add("K12_NATIVE_EMERGENCE_PROMOTION", lambda item, _rows: item.__setitem__(
   635	        "overall_correspondence_status", "NATIVE_CARRIER_DERIVED"
   636	    ))
   637	    add("K13_MISSING_DIRECT_SOURCE_LINEAGE", lambda _item, rows: rows.__setitem__(
   638	        slice(None), [row for row in rows if row["path"] not in DIRECT_SOURCES]
   639	    ))
   640	    add("K14_MISSING_EDGE_COMPARISONS", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   641	        "matched_edge_transport_comparisons", 0
   642	    ))
   643	    add("K15_INTRINSIC_COVARIANCE_FAILURE", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   644	        "maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual", 1.0e9
   645	    ))
   646	    add("K16_CONTINUOUS_BUNDLE_PROMOTION", lambda item, _rows: item.__setitem__(
   647	        "sampled_path_status", "CONTINUOUS_BUNDLE_THEOREM"
   648	    ))
   649	    add("K17_SYMBOLIC_ANGULAR_GAP_MUTATION", lambda item, _rows: item["symbolic_toric"].__setitem__(
   650	        "angular_gap", "nonsense"
   651	    ))
   652	    add("K18_HOPF_SEED_SOURCE_MUTATION", lambda item, _rows: item["direct_hopf_seed"].__setitem__(
   653	        "source_sha256", "0" * 64
   654	    ))
   655	    add("K19_HOPF_SEED_SAMPLE_COUNT_MUTATION", lambda item, _rows: item["direct_hopf_seed"].__setitem__(
   656	        "sample_points", 1
   657	    ))
   658	    add("K20_UNCERTAINTY_ACCOUNTING_LOSS", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   659	        "uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons", 0
   660	    ))
   661	    add("K21_SKIPPED_EDGE_ACCOUNTING_LOSS", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   662	        "skipped_edge_transport_comparisons", 0
   663	    ))
   664	    add("K22_FIXED_JACOBIAN_SUBSTITUTION", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   665	        "coordinate_map_interpretation", "FIXED_JACOBIAN"
   666	    ))
   667	    add("K23_SYMBOLIC_CONNECTION_MUTATION", lambda item, _rows: item["symbolic_toric"].__setitem__(
   668	        "diagonal_connection_weight", "nonsense"
   669	    ))
   670	    def redistribute_point_status(item, _rows):
   671	        item["covariance"]["point_status_census"] = {
   672	            "BOTH_CLASSIFIED": 67395,
   673	            "ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN": 34,
   674	            "BOTH_UNCERTAIN": 27,
   675	        }
   676	        item["covariance"]["uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons"] = 61
   677	
   678	    add("K24_COORDINATED_POINT_CENSUS_REDISTRIBUTION", redistribute_point_status)
   679	
   680	    def replace_edge_split(item, _rows):
   681	        item["covariance"]["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"] = 1
   682	        item["covariance"]["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"] = 63487
   683	        item["covariance"]["skipped_edge_reason_census"] = {"FABRICATED_REASON": 63487}
   684	
   685	    add("K25_COORDINATED_EDGE_SPLIT_AND_REASON_REPLACEMENT", replace_edge_split)
   686	    add("K26_NEGATIVE_RESIDUAL", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   687	        "maximum_intrinsic_object_covariance_residual", -1.0
   688	    ))
   689	    add("K27_FABRICATED_SEED_SOURCE_PATH", lambda item, _rows: item["direct_hopf_seed"].__setitem__(
   690	        "source_path", "fabricated.py"
   691	    ))
   692	    add("K28_NEGATIVE_POINT_STATUS_COUNT", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   693	        "point_status_census", {
   694	            "BOTH_CLASSIFIED": 67457,
   695	            "ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN": -1,
   696	            "BOTH_UNCERTAIN": 0,
   697	        }
   698	    ))
   699	    add("K29_NONFINITE_JACOBIAN_DETERMINANT", lambda item, _rows: item["covariance"].__setitem__(
   700	        "minimum_absolute_jacobian_determinant", math.inf
   701	    ))
   702	    return mutations

   705	def main() -> None:
   706	    covariance = covariance_audit()
   707	    symbolic = symbolic_toric_audit()
   708	    seed = direct_hopf_seed_audit()
   709	    result = {
   710	        "schema": "udt-motif-hopf-review-correction-1.0",
   711	        "status": "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE",
   712	        "covariance": covariance,
   713	        "frobenius_certification_scope": "REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY",
   714	        "symbolic_toric": symbolic,
   715	        "direct_hopf_seed": seed,
   716	        "construction_provenance": {
   717	            "supplied_equal_weight_circle_action": True,
   718	            "imported_s2_matter_carrier": False,
   719	            "imported_l2_l4_action_functional": False,
   720	        },
   721	        "sampled_path_status": SAMPLED_STATUS,
   722	        "overall_correspondence_status": "LEAD",
   723	        "maximum_conclusion": MAXIMUM,
   724	    }
   725	    lineage = read_tsv(HERE / "SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv")
   726	    validate_result(result, lineage)
   727	    catches = mutation_catches(result, lineage)
   728	    result["exercised_mutation_catches"] = len(catches)
   729	    with (HERE / "REVIEW_CORRECTION_CATCH_PROOFS.tsv").open(
   730	        "w", encoding="utf-8", newline=""
   731	    ) as handle:
   732	        writer = csv.DictWriter(
   733	            handle, fieldnames=("catch_id", "result"), delimiter="\t", lineterminator="\n"
   734	        )
   735	        writer.writeheader()
   736	        writer.writerows(catches)
   737	    (HERE / "REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json").write_text(
   738	        json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8"
   739	    )
   740	    print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True))
   741	
   742	
   743	if __name__ == "__main__":
   744	    main()
