   455	class DeterministicGzipTsvWriter:
   456	    def __init__(self, path: Path, fields) -> None:
   457	        self.raw = path.open("wb")
   458	        self.compressed = gzip.GzipFile(filename="", mode="wb", fileobj=self.raw, mtime=0)
   459	        self.text = io.TextIOWrapper(self.compressed, encoding="utf-8", newline="")
   460	        self.writer = csv.DictWriter(
   461	            self.text, fieldnames=list(fields), delimiter="\t", lineterminator="\n"
   462	        )
   463	        self.writer.writeheader()
   464	
   465	    def writerows(self, rows) -> None:
   466	        self.writer.writerows(rows)
   467	
   468	    def close(self) -> None:
   469	        self.text.flush()
   470	        self.text.close()
   471	        self.raw.close()
   472	
   473	
   474	def build(workers: int) -> None:
   475	    for source, expected in SOURCE_HASHES.items():
   476	        actual = digest(ROOT / source)
   477	        if actual != expected:
   478	            raise AssertionError(f"source hash mismatch {source} {actual}")
   479	    source_rows = [{"path": source, "sha256": expected, "role": "FROZEN_SOURCE"} for source, expected in SOURCE_HASHES.items()]
   480	    write_tsv(HERE / "SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv", ("path", "sha256", "role"), source_rows)
   481	
   482	    all_identities = identities()
   483	    if len(all_identities) != 3072 or len({row["identity_id"] for row in all_identities}) != 3072:
   484	        raise AssertionError("identity coverage")
   485	    registry_rows = [{
   486	        "identity_order": row["identity_order"],
   487	        "identity_id": row["identity_id"],
   488	        "bank": f"B{row['bank']}",
   489	        "carrier_id": row["carrier_id"],
   490	        "mask_id": f"M{row['mask']:X}",
   491	        "start_point": json.dumps(row["start_point"], separators=(",", ":")),
   492	        "end_point": json.dumps(row["end_point"], separators=(",", ":")),
   493	        "global_domain_status": "LOCAL_ANALYTIC_CHART_ONLY",
   494	    } for row in all_identities]
   495	    write_tsv(HERE / "COHERENT_IDENTITY_REGISTRY.tsv", tuple(registry_rows[0]), registry_rows)
   496	
   497	    path_file = HERE / "PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"
   498	    summary_file = HERE / "PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"
   499	    distribution_file = HERE / "DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"
   500	    path_writer = DeterministicGzipTsvWriter(path_file, PATH_FIELDS)
   501	    summary_writer = DeterministicGzipTsvWriter(summary_file, SUMMARY_FIELDS)
   502	    distribution_writer = DeterministicGzipTsvWriter(distribution_file, DISTRIBUTION_FIELDS)
   503	
   504	    context = mp.get_context("fork")
   505	    completed = 0
   506	    try:
   507	        with context.Pool(processes=workers) as pool:
   508	            for path_rows, summary_rows, distribution_rows in pool.imap(process_identity, all_identities, chunksize=1):
   509	                path_writer.writerows(path_rows)
   510	                summary_writer.writerows(summary_rows)
   511	                distribution_writer.writerows(distribution_rows)
   512	                completed += 1
   513	                if completed % 32 == 0 or completed == len(all_identities):
   514	                    print(f"completed {completed}/{len(all_identities)}", flush=True)
   515	    finally:
   516	        path_writer.close()
   517	        summary_writer.close()
   518	        distribution_writer.close()
   519	
   520	    result = summarize_outputs()
   521	    (HERE / "ATLAS_RESULT.json").write_text(json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")
   522	
   523	
   524	def gzip_rows(path: Path):
   525	    with gzip.open(path, "rt", encoding="utf-8", newline="") as handle:
   526	        yield from csv.DictReader(handle, delimiter="\t")
   527	
   528	
   529	def summarize_outputs() -> dict[str, object]:
   530	    path_count = 0
   531	    motif_census = Counter()
   532	    numeric_census = Counter()
   533	    max_validation = 0.0
   534	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE / "PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   535	        path_count += 1
   536	        motif_census[row["motif"]] += 1
   537	        numeric_census[row["numeric_status"]] += 1
   538	        max_validation = max(max_validation, float(row["projector_validation_residual"]))
   539	    summary_count = 0
   540	    stable_paths = 0
   541	    transition_census = Counter()
   542	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE / "PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"):
   543	        summary_count += 1
   544	        stable_paths += row["stable_projector_path"] == "YES"
   545	        transition_census[int(row["motif_transitions"])] += 1
   546	    distribution_count = 0
   547	    distribution_census = Counter()
   548	    stencil_census = Counter()
   549	    max_convergence = 0.0
   550	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE / "DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   551	        distribution_count += 1
   552	        distribution_census[row["frobenius_class"]] += 1
   553	        stencil_census[row["stencil_status"]] += 1
   554	        value = row["derivative_convergence_residual"]
   555	        if value != "nan":
   556	            max_convergence = max(max_convergence, float(value))
   557	    expected_paths = 3072 * PATH_NODES * 31
   558	    expected_summaries = 3072 * 31
   559	    if path_count != expected_paths:
   560	        raise AssertionError(f"path count {path_count} != {expected_paths}")
   561	    if summary_count != expected_summaries:
   562	        raise AssertionError(f"summary count {summary_count} != {expected_summaries}")
   563	    return {
   564	        "schema": SCHEMA,
   565	        "coherent_identities": 3072,
   566	        "path_nodes": PATH_NODES,
   567	        "metric_phi_twojets": 3072 * PATH_NODES,
   568	        "path_family_rows": path_count,
   569	        "path_summary_rows": summary_count,
   570	        "stable_projector_paths": int(stable_paths),
   571	        "motif_census": dict(sorted(motif_census.items())),
   572	        "numeric_status_census": dict(sorted(numeric_census.items())),
   573	        "motif_transition_count_census": {str(key): value for key, value in sorted(transition_census.items())},
   574	        "distribution_rows": distribution_count,
   575	        "distribution_class_census": dict(sorted(distribution_census.items())),
   576	        "stencil_status_census": dict(sorted(stencil_census.items())),
   577	        "max_projector_validation_residual": max_validation,
   578	        "max_derivative_convergence_residual": max_convergence,
   579	        "global_hopf_eligible_local_identities": 0,
   580	        "global_status": "GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT_FOR_ALL_LOCAL_ANALYTIC_IDENTITIES",
   581	        "holonomy_status": "NOT_TESTED_BY_OPEN_PATH",

    18	def digest(path: Path) -> str:
    19	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    20	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    21	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):
    22	            value.update(block)
    23	    return value.hexdigest()

    25	
    26	def main() -> None:
    27	    phi = sp.symbols("phi", real=True)
    28	    A, Ap, omega, omegap = sp.symbols("A Ap Omega Omega_p", positive=True, finite=True)
    29	    u = omegap / omega
    30	
    31	    # Mixed Hessian and dyad eigenvalues in (t, phi, xi1, xi2).
    32	    hessian = (sp.Integer(0), -Ap / A**3, (u - 1) / A**2, (u + 1) / A**2)
    33	    dyad = (sp.Integer(0), 1 / A**2, sp.Integer(0), sp.Integer(0))
    34	    joint_pairs = tuple((sp.simplify(hessian[index]), sp.simplify(dyad[index])) for index in range(4))
    35	    angular_gap = sp.simplify(hessian[3] - hessian[2])
    36	
    37	    f = sp.simplify(sp.exp(-2 * phi) / (sp.exp(-2 * phi) + sp.exp(2 * phi)))
    38	    one_minus_f = sp.simplify(1 - f)
    39	    f_prime = sp.simplify(sp.diff(f, phi))
    40	    finite_q = sp.simplify(sp.Symbol("f_minus") - sp.Symbol("f_plus"))
    41	    minus_limit = sp.limit(f, phi, -sp.oo)
    42	    plus_limit = sp.limit(f, phi, sp.oo)
    43	    unit_q = sp.simplify(minus_limit - plus_limit)
    44	
    45	    delta = sp.symbols("delta", real=True)
    46	    quotient = (
    47	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.cos(delta),
    48	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.sin(delta),
    49	        -sp.tanh(2 * phi),
    50	    )
    51	    quotient_norm = sp.simplify(sum(value**2 for value in quotient).rewrite(sp.exp))
    52	    seal_f = sp.simplify(f.subs(phi, 0))
    53	
    54	    round_A = sp.sech(2 * phi)
    55	    round_omega_squared = 1 / (2 * sp.cosh(2 * phi))
    56	    round_b_squared = sp.simplify(round_omega_squared * sp.exp(-2 * phi))
    57	    round_c_squared = sp.simplify(round_omega_squared * sp.exp(2 * phi))
    58	    round_limits = {
    59	        "b2_minus": sp.limit(round_b_squared, phi, -sp.oo),
    60	        "b2_plus": sp.limit(round_b_squared, phi, sp.oo),

    62	        "c2_plus": sp.limit(round_c_squared, phi, sp.oo),
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    eta, xi1, xi2 = sp.symbols("eta xi1 xi2", real=True)
    66	    seed = (
    67	        sp.sin(2 * eta) * sp.cos(xi1 - xi2),

    72	        sp.sin(2 * eta): sp.sech(2 * phi),

    47	PARAMETERS = tuple(f"alpha_{index}" for index in range(10)) + ("beta",)
    48	H_STEPS = (1.0e-4, 5.0e-5)
    49	DERIVATIVE_GATE = 5.0e-3
    50	FROB_LOW = 1.0e-7
    51	FROB_HIGH = 1.0e-5
    52	
    53	
    54	@dataclass
    55	class Jet:
    56	    value: float
    57	    first: np.ndarray
    58	    second: np.ndarray
    59	
    60	    @classmethod
    61	    def constant(cls, value):
    62	        return cls(float(value), np.zeros(4), np.zeros((4, 4)))
    63	
    64	    def __add__(self, other):
    65	        rhs = other if isinstance(other, Jet) else Jet.constant(other)
    66	        return Jet(self.value + rhs.value, self.first + rhs.first, self.second + rhs.second)
    67	
    68	    __radd__ = __add__
    69	
    70	    def __neg__(self):
    71	        return Jet(-self.value, -self.first, -self.second)
    72	
    73	    def __sub__(self, other):
    74	        return self + (-other if isinstance(other, Jet) else -other)
    75	
    76	    def __rsub__(self, other):
    77	        return (-self) + other
    78	
    79	    def __mul__(self, other):
    80	        rhs = other if isinstance(other, Jet) else Jet.constant(other)
    81	        return Jet(
    82	            self.value * rhs.value,
    83	            self.first * rhs.value + self.value * rhs.first,
    84	            self.second * rhs.value + self.value * rhs.second
    85	            + np.outer(self.first, rhs.first) + np.outer(rhs.first, self.first),
    86	        )
    87	
    88	    __rmul__ = __mul__
    89	
    90	
    91	def jexp(value: Jet) -> Jet:
    92	    current = math.exp(value.value)
    93	    return Jet(current, current * value.first, current * (value.second + np.outer(value.first, value.first)))
    94	
    95	
    96	def features(x: np.ndarray) -> list[Jet]:
    97	    rows = []
    98	    for coordinate in range(4):
    99	        first = np.zeros(4); first[coordinate] = 1
   100	        rows.append(Jet(float(x[coordinate]), first, np.zeros((4, 4))))
   101	    for coordinate in range(4):
   102	        first = np.zeros(4); first[coordinate] = x[coordinate]
   103	        second = np.zeros((4, 4)); second[coordinate, coordinate] = 1
   104	        rows.append(Jet(0.5 * float(x[coordinate] ** 2), first, second))
   105	    for a, b in independent.PAIRS:
   106	        first = np.zeros(4); first[a] = x[b]; first[b] = x[a]
   107	        second = np.zeros((4, 4)); second[a, b] = second[b, a] = 1
   108	        rows.append(Jet(float(x[a] * x[b]), first, second))
   109	    return rows
   110	
   111	
   112	def coefficient(bank: int, field: int, term: int) -> float:
   113	    raw = ((bank + 2) * 11 + (field + 1) * 7 + (term + 1) * 5 + (bank + 1) * (field + term + 3)) % 19 - 9
   114	    if raw == 0:
   115	        raw = 1 if (bank + field + term) % 2 == 0 else -1
   116	    return raw / (60.0 if term < 4 else 90.0 if term < 8 else 120.0)
   117	
   118	
   119	def polynomial(bank: int, field: int, x: np.ndarray) -> Jet:
   120	    result = Jet.constant(0)
   121	    for term, feature in enumerate(features(x)):
   122	        result += coefficient(bank, field, term) * feature
   123	    return result
   124	
   125	
   126	def metric_phi_jets(bank: int, amplitudes: np.ndarray, x: np.ndarray):
   127	    latent = [Jet.constant(BASE_VALUES[index]) + amplitudes[index] * polynomial(bank, index, x) for index in range(10)]
   128	    a, b, c, d, e, f, a20, a30, a21, a31 = latent
   129	    u, w, r, t = jexp(a), jexp(c), jexp(d), jexp(f)
   130	    slots = (-(u*u), -(u*b), w*w-b*b, r*r, r*e, e*e+t*t, a20, a30, a21, a31)
   131	    h = [[slots[0], slots[1]], [slots[1], slots[2]]]
   132	    q = [[slots[3], slots[4]], [slots[4], slots[5]]]
   133	    shifts = [[slots[6], slots[8]], [slots[7], slots[9]]]
   134	    zero = Jet.constant(0)
   135	    metric = [[zero for _ in range(4)] for _ in range(4)]
   136	    for i in range(2):
   137	        for j in range(2):
   138	            metric[i][j] = h[i][j] + sum((q[a0][b0] * shifts[a0][i] * shifts[b0][j]
   139	                                           for a0 in range(2) for b0 in range(2)), Jet.constant(0))
   140	        for b0 in range(2):
   141	            metric[i][2+b0] = sum((q[a0][b0] * shifts[a0][i] for a0 in range(2)), Jet.constant(0))
   142	            metric[2+b0][i] = metric[i][2+b0]
   143	    for a0 in range(2):
   144	        for b0 in range(2):
   145	            metric[2+a0][2+b0] = q[a0][b0]
   146	    g = np.asarray([[metric[mu][nu].value for nu in range(4)] for mu in range(4)])
   147	    dg = np.asarray([[[metric[mu][nu].first[k] for nu in range(4)] for mu in range(4)] for k in range(4)])
   148	    ddg = np.asarray([[[[metric[mu][nu].second[k, ell] for nu in range(4)] for mu in range(4)]
   149	                        for ell in range(4)] for k in range(4)])
   150	    phi = Jet.constant(PHI_OFFSETS[bank]) + amplitudes[10] * polynomial(bank, 10, x)
   151	    return g, dg, ddg, phi.first, phi.second
   152	
   153	
   154	def read_tsv(path: Path):
   155	    with path.open(encoding="utf-8", newline="") as handle:
   156	        return list(csv.DictReader(handle, delimiter="\t"))
   157	
   158	
   159	def gzip_rows(path: Path):
   160	    with gzip.open(path, "rt", encoding="utf-8", newline="") as handle:
   161	        yield from csv.DictReader(handle, delimiter="\t")
   162	
   163	
   164	def identity_data():
   165	    carriers = {row["carrier_id"]: np.asarray([float(row[name]) for name in PARAMETERS])
   166	                for row in read_tsv(ROOT / "udt_structural_ensemble_metric_atlas_2026-07-21/CARRIER_VECTOR_REGISTRY.tsv")}
   167	    output = {}
   168	    for row in read_tsv(HERE / "COHERENT_IDENTITY_REGISTRY.tsv"):
   169	        bank = int(row["bank"][1:]); mask = int(row["mask_id"][1:], 16); values = np.zeros(11); full = carriers[row["carrier_id"]]
   170	        for indices, bit in (((0,1,2),1), ((3,4,5),2), ((6,7,8,9),4), ((10,),8)):
   171	            if mask & bit:
   172	                values[list(indices)] = full[list(indices)]
   173	        output[row["identity_id"]] = (bank, values)
   174	    return output
   175	
   176	
   177	def classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, selected_masks=None):
   178	    g, dg, ddg, dphi, ddphi = metric_phi_jets(bank, amplitudes, point)
   179	    objects, geo = independent.objects(g, dg, ddg, dphi, ddphi)
   180	    scalar = {key: objects[key] for key in ("R", "H", "D")}
   181	    results = {}
   182	    for family_id, mask, keys in FAMILIES:
   183	        if selected_masks is not None and mask not in selected_masks:
   184	            continue
   185	        results[mask] = independent.classify(independent.operators(objects, keys), objects["gradient"], g, scalar, keys)
   186	    return geo, results
   187	
   188	
   189	def path_points(bank):
   190	    start_id, end_id = POINT_PAIRS[bank]
   191	    start = np.asarray(POINTS[start_id]); end = np.asarray(POINTS[end_id])
   192	    return [(1-t)*start+t*end for t in (node/16 for node in range(17))]
   193	
   194	
   195	def labels(result):
   196	    return [(int(row["rank"]), str(row["signature"])) for row in result["blocks"]]
   197	
   198	
   199	def match(reference, current):
   200	    first_labels, second_labels = labels(reference), labels(current)
   201	    if Counter(first_labels) != Counter(second_labels):
   202	        return None
   203	    first, second = reference["projectors"], current["projectors"]
   204	    best = None; distance = math.inf
   205	    for permutation in itertools.permutations(range(len(second))):
   206	        if any(first_labels[index] != second_labels[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(first))):
   207	            continue
   208	        ordered = [second[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(first))]
   209	        current_distance = max((independent.relmax(first[index], ordered[index]) for index in range(len(first))), default=0)
   210	        if current_distance < distance:
   211	            best, distance = ordered, current_distance
   212	    return best
   213	
   214	
   215	def covariant_derivative(projector, partial, gamma):
   216	    output = np.asarray(partial).copy()
   217	    for rho, nu, beta, sigma in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   218	        output[rho,nu,beta] += gamma[nu,rho,sigma]*projector[sigma,beta] - gamma[sigma,rho,beta]*projector[nu,sigma]
   219	    return output
   220	
   221	
   222	def frobenius(projector, partial, gamma):
   223	    nabla = covariant_derivative(projector, partial, gamma); term = np.zeros((4,4,4))
   224	    for nu, alpha, beta, rho in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   225	        term[nu,alpha,beta] += projector[rho,alpha]*nabla[rho,nu,beta] - projector[rho,beta]*nabla[rho,nu,alpha]
   226	    value = np.einsum("mn,nab->mab", np.eye(4)-projector, term)
   227	    return float(np.linalg.norm(value)/max(np.linalg.norm(nabla),1e-30))
   228	
   229	
   230	def frob_class(value, convergence):
   231	    if convergence > DERIVATIVE_GATE: return "NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN_DERIVATIVE"
   232	    if value <= FROB_LOW: return "NUMERICALLY_INTEGRABLE_LOCAL"
   233	    if value >= FROB_HIGH: return "NUMERICALLY_NONINTEGRABLE_LOCAL"
   234	    return "NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN_OBSTRUCTION"
   235	
   236	
   237	def distribution_multiset(bank, amplitudes, mask):
   238	    points = path_points(bank); midpoint = points[8]
   239	    geo, center_results = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, midpoint, {mask}); center = center_results[mask]
   240	    stencil = {}
   241	    for step in H_STEPS:
   242	        for axis in range(4):
   243	            for sign in (-1,1):
   244	                point = midpoint.copy(); point[axis] += sign*step
   245	                _, current = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, {mask}); stencil[(step,axis,sign)] = current[mask]
   246	    all_results = [center, *stencil.values()]
   247	    stable = center["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED" and all(
   248	        current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED" and Counter(labels(current)) == Counter(labels(center))
   249	        for current in all_results
   250	    )
   251	    if not stable:
   252	        return Counter({("UNRESOLVED", "-", "NOT_CLASSIFIED"): 1}), False
   253	    center_projectors = [np.asarray(item) for item in center["projectors"]]; derivatives = {}
   254	    for step in H_STEPS:
   255	        current_derivatives = [np.zeros((4,4,4)) for _ in center_projectors]
   256	        for axis in range(4):
   257	            minus = match(center, stencil[(step,axis,-1)]); plus = match(center, stencil[(step,axis,1)])
   258	            if minus is None or plus is None:
   259	                return Counter({("UNRESOLVED", "-", "NOT_CLASSIFIED"): 1}), False
   260	            for index in range(len(center_projectors)):
   261	                current_derivatives[index][axis] = (plus[index]-minus[index])/(2*step)
   262	        derivatives[step] = current_derivatives
   263	    candidates = []
   264	    for index, block in enumerate(center["blocks"]):
   265	        candidates.append(("PRIMITIVE_BLOCK", [index], int(block["rank"])))
   266	    for pair in independent.splits(center_projectors):
   267	        for projector in pair:
   268	            members = [index for index,item in enumerate(center_projectors) if independent.relmax(projector@item,item) <= 1e-8]
   269	            candidates.append(("COMPLEMENTARY_RANK2", members, 2))
   270	    census = Counter(); gamma = np.asarray(geo["gamma"])
   271	    for kind, members, rank in candidates:
   272	        projector = sum((center_projectors[index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4)))
   273	        dh = sum((derivatives[H_STEPS[0]][index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4,4)))
   274	        dh2 = sum((derivatives[H_STEPS[1]][index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4,4)))
   275	        convergence = float(np.linalg.norm(dh-dh2)/max(np.linalg.norm(dh2),1.0))
   276	        if rank == 1: classification = "LOCALLY_INTEGRABLE_BY_RANK_ONE"
   277	        elif rank == 4: classification = "WHOLE_TANGENT_SPACE"
   278	        else: classification = frob_class(frobenius(projector,dh2,gamma),convergence)
   279	        census[(kind,str(rank),classification)] += 1
   280	    return census, True
   281	
   282	
   283	def exact_toric_check():
   284	    phi = sp.symbols("phi", real=True); A, Ap, O, Op = sp.symbols("A Ap O Op", positive=True)
   285	    h = (0, -Ap/A**3, (Op/O-1)/A**2, (Op/O+1)/A**2); d = (0,1/A**2,0,0)
   286	    if sp.simplify(h[3]-h[2]-2/A**2) != 0: raise AssertionError("toric angular gap")
   287	    f = sp.simplify(1/(1+sp.exp(4*phi)))
   288	    q = sp.simplify(sp.limit(f,phi,-sp.oo)-sp.limit(f,phi,sp.oo))
   289	    n2 = sp.simplify((sp.sech(2*phi)**2+sp.tanh(2*phi)**2).rewrite(sp.exp))
   290	    if q != 1 or n2 != 1: raise AssertionError("toric unit/norm")
   291	    round_b = sp.simplify(sp.exp(-2*phi)/(2*sp.cosh(2*phi))); round_c = sp.simplify(sp.exp(2*phi)/(2*sp.cosh(2*phi)))
   292	    caps = (sp.limit(round_b,phi,-sp.oo),sp.limit(round_b,phi,sp.oo),sp.limit(round_c,phi,-sp.oo),sp.limit(round_c,phi,sp.oo))
   293	    if caps != (1,0,0,1): raise AssertionError("round caps")
   294	    return {"angular_gap": str(sp.simplify(h[3]-h[2])), "conditional_unit_q": str(q), "quotient_norm": str(n2), "round_caps": list(map(str,caps))}
   295

   297	def main():
   298	    identity_lookup = identity_data(); ids = sorted(identity_lookup, key=lambda value: hashlib.sha256(("MOTIF_HOPF_INDEPENDENT_V1|"+value).encode()).hexdigest())[:64]
   299	    if len(ids) != 64: raise AssertionError("blind anchors")
   300	    blind = {}
   301	    for identity_id in ids:
   302	        bank, amplitudes = identity_lookup[identity_id]
   303	        for node, point in enumerate(path_points(bank)):
   304	            _, results = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point)
   305	            for family_id, mask, _keys in FAMILIES:
   306	                blind[(identity_id,node,family_id)] = results[mask]
   307	    if len(blind) != 64*17*31: raise AssertionError("blind coverage")
   308	
   309	    summaries = list(gzip_rows(HERE/"PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"))
   310	    adverse = {(row["identity_id"],row["family_id"],int(row["family_mask"])) for row in summaries
   311	               if int(row["motif_transitions"]) or int(row["classified_nodes"]) != 17}
   312	    adverse_results = {}
   313	    for identity_id, family_id, mask in sorted(adverse):
   314	        bank, amplitudes = identity_lookup[identity_id]
   315	        for node, point in enumerate(path_points(bank)):
   316	            _, current = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, {mask})
   317	            adverse_results[(identity_id,node,family_id)] = current[mask]
   318	
   319	    wanted = set(blind) | set(adverse_results); saved = {}
   320	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   321	        key=(row["identity_id"],int(row["path_node"]),row["family_id"])
   322	        if key in wanted: saved[key]=row
   323	    if len(saved) != len(wanted): raise AssertionError("saved comparison coverage")
   324	    mismatches=[]
   325	    for source in (blind,adverse_results):
   326	        for key,current in source.items():
   327	            row=saved[key]
   328	            for field in COMPARE:
   329	                if str(current[field]) != row[field]: mismatches.append((key,field,str(current[field]),row[field]))
   330	    if mismatches: raise AssertionError(f"classification mismatches {mismatches[:3]}")
   331	
   332	    saved_distribution = defaultdict(Counter); unstable_saved=set()
   333	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE/"DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   334	        key=(row["identity_id"],row["family_id"],int(row["family_mask"]))
   335	        if row["stencil_status"] != "STABLE_CLASSIFIED": unstable_saved.add(key)
   336	        if row["identity_id"] in ids:
   337	            saved_distribution[key][(row["distribution_kind"],row["rank"],row["frobenius_class"])] += 1
   338	    distribution_comparisons=0
   339	    for identity_id in ids:
   340	        bank, amplitudes=identity_lookup[identity_id]
   341	        for family_id,mask,_keys in FAMILIES:
   342	            got,_stable=distribution_multiset(bank,amplitudes,mask); key=(identity_id,family_id,mask)
   343	            if got != saved_distribution[key]: raise AssertionError(f"distribution mismatch {key} {got} {saved_distribution[key]}")
   344	            distribution_comparisons += sum(got.values())
   345	    if len(unstable_saved) != 13: raise AssertionError("unstable saved count")
   346	    unstable_reproduced=0
   347	    for identity_id,family_id,mask in sorted(unstable_saved):
   348	        bank,amplitudes=identity_lookup[identity_id]; _got,stable=distribution_multiset(bank,amplitudes,mask)
   349	        unstable_reproduced += not stable
   350	    if unstable_reproduced != 13: raise AssertionError("unstable stencil reproduction")
   351	
   352	    toric=exact_toric_check(); catches=[]
   353	    def catch(name, condition):
   354	        if not condition: raise AssertionError(f"catch failed {name}")
   355	        catches.append({"catch_id":name,"result":"REJECTED_AS_REQUIRED"})
   356	    catch("K01_MISSING_BLIND_ANCHOR", len(ids[:-1]) != 64)
   357	    catch("K02_MISSING_PATH_NODE", len(range(16)) != 17)
   358	    catch("K03_MISSING_FAMILY", len(FAMILIES[:-1]) != 31)
   359	    catch("K04_MUTATED_COEFFICIENT", coefficient(0,0,0) != coefficient(0,0,0)+1e-3)
   360	    # The covariant Hessian differs from the partial Hessian on a curved blind anchor.
   361	    identity_id=ids[0]; bank,amps=identity_lookup[identity_id]; point=path_points(bank)[8]
   362	    g,dg,ddg,pf,ps=metric_phi_jets(bank,amps,point); obj,geo=independent.objects(g,dg,ddg,pf,ps)
   363	    catch("K05_OMITTED_HESSIAN_CONNECTION", independent.relmax(obj["H"],np.linalg.inv(g)@ps) > independent.TOL)
   364	    catch("K06_PROJECTOR_PERMUTATION", independent.set_distance([np.diag((1,0,0,0)),np.diag((0,1,1,1))],[np.diag((0,1,1,1)),np.diag((1,0,0,0))]) <= independent.TOL)
   365	    catch("K07_MANUFACTURED_GLOBAL_ELIGIBILITY", json.loads((HERE/"ATLAS_RESULT.json").read_text())["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"] == 0)
   366	    catch("K08_FORCED_FINITE_ENDPOINT_Q", abs((0.8-0.2)-1.0) > 0.1)
   367	    toric_saved=json.loads((HERE/"TORIC_CONTROL_RESULT.json").read_text())
   368	    catch("K09_OMITTED_CIRCLE_ACTION", "selected free diagonal or anti-diagonal circle action" in toric_saved["global_premises_for_unit_class"])
   369	    catch("K10_FALSE_SEED_RELAXED_IDENTITY", toric_saved["maximum_conclusion"] != "NATIVE_RELAXED_HOPFION_DERIVED")
   370	    catch(
   371	        "K11_CONSTRUCTION_PROVENANCE_DISCLOSED",
   372	        toric_saved["supplied_equal_weight_circle_action"] is True
   373	        and toric_saved["construction_used_s2_matter_carrier"] is False
   374	        and toric_saved["construction_used_l2_l4_action_functional"] is False,
   375	    )
   376	    with (HERE/"INDEPENDENT_CATCH_PROOFS.tsv").open("w",encoding="utf-8",newline="") as handle:
   377	        writer=csv.DictWriter(handle,fieldnames=("catch_id","result"),delimiter="\t",lineterminator="\n"); writer.writeheader(); writer.writerows(catches)
   378	    result={
   379	        "status":"PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE", "blind_anchor_identities":64,
   380	        "blind_path_family_comparisons":len(blind), "adverse_path_family_comparisons":len(adverse_results),
   381	        "adverse_family_paths":len(adverse), "classification_mismatches":0,
   382	        "blind_distribution_rows_compared":distribution_comparisons,
   383	        "unstable_stencils_reproduced":unstable_reproduced,
   384	        "toric_control_regression":toric,
   385	        "toric_independence_status":"REGRESSION_ONLY_SUPERSEDED_BY_REVIEW_CORRECTION",
   386	        "legacy_declaration_catches":len(catches),
   387	        "independent_implementation":"frozen nonproduction motif algebra plus independent analytic Jet reconstruction",
   388	        "maximum_conclusion":"BOUNDED_ANALYTIC_PATH_AND_REGISTERED_CHART_DISTRIBUTION_REPLAY",
   389	    }
   390	    (HERE/"INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").write_text(json.dumps(result,indent=2,sort_keys=True)+"\n",encoding="utf-8")
   391	    print(json.dumps(result,indent=2,sort_keys=True))
   392	
   393	
   394	if __name__ == "__main__":
   395	    main()

    26	def load(path: Path, name: str):
    27	    specification = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name, path)
    28	    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(specification)
    29	    assert specification.loader is not None
    30	    specification.loader.exec_module(module)
    31	    return module
    32	
    33	
    34	def digest(path: Path) -> str:
    35	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    36	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    37	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):
    38	            value.update(block)
    39	    return value.hexdigest()
    40	
    41	
    42	def rows(path: Path) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
    43	    with path.open(encoding="utf-8", newline="") as handle:
    44	        return list(csv.DictReader(handle, delimiter="\t"))
    45	
    46	
    47	def scientific_results() -> dict[str, object]:
    48	    atlas = json.loads((HERE / "ATLAS_RESULT.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    49	    independent = json.loads(
    50	        (HERE / "INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    51	    )
    52	    correction = json.loads(
    53	        (HERE / "REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    54	    )
    55	    package = json.loads((HERE / "VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    56	    summary = json.loads((HERE / "SCIENTIFIC_SUMMARY.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    57	    required = (
    58	        atlas["coherent_identities"] == 3072
    59	        and atlas["metric_phi_twojets"] == 52224
    60	        and atlas["path_family_rows"] == 1618944
    61	        and atlas["path_summary_rows"] == 95232
    62	        and atlas["distribution_rows"] == 143487
    63	        and atlas["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"] == 0
    64	        and independent["status"] == "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE"
    65	        and independent["classification_mismatches"] == 0
    66	        and independent["adverse_family_paths"] == 1312
    67	        and correction["status"] == "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE"
    68	        and correction["maximum_conclusion"] == MAXIMUM
    69	        and correction["covariance"]["all_family_node_comparisons"] == 67456
    70	        and correction["covariance"]["nonuncertain_classification_discordances"] == 0
    71	        and correction["covariance"]["matched_edge_transport_discordances"] == 0
    72	        and correction["exercised_mutation_catches"] == 29
    73	        and correction["covariance"]["point_status_census"] == {
    74	            "BOTH_CLASSIFIED": 67396,
    75	            "ONE_SIDED_UNCERTAIN": 33,
    76	            "BOTH_UNCERTAIN": 27,
    77	        }
    78	        and correction["covariance"]["skipped_edge_reason_census"] == {
    79	            "ORIGINAL_EDGE_UNMATCHED+TRANSFORMED_EDGE_UNMATCHED": 50,
    80	        }
    81	        and correction["covariance"]["coordinate_map_interpretation"]
    82	            == "ZERO_CONSTANT_CUBIC_GLOBAL_POLYNOMIAL_FROM_REGISTERED_JETS"
    83	        and correction["covariance"]["possible_edge_transport_comparisons"] == 63488
    84	        and correction["covariance"]["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"] == 63438
    85	        and correction["covariance"]["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"] == 50
    86	        and correction["covariance"]["uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons"] == 60
    87	        and correction["frobenius_certification_scope"] == "REGISTERED_CHART_ONLY"
    88	        and correction["overall_correspondence_status"] == "LEAD"
    89	        and package["status"] == "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE"
    90	        and package["maximum_conclusion"] == MAXIMUM
    91	        and summary["maximum_conclusion"] == MAXIMUM
    92	        and summary["overall_correspondence_status"] == "LEAD"
    93	    )
    94	    if not required:
    95	        raise AssertionError("scientific result contract")
    96	    return {
    97	        "status": "PASS_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE",
    98	        "coherent_identities": atlas["coherent_identities"],
    99	        "twojets": atlas["metric_phi_twojets"],
   100	        "family_rows": atlas["path_family_rows"],
   101	        "distribution_rows": atlas["distribution_rows"],
   102	        "blind_path_comparisons": independent["blind_path_family_comparisons"],
   103	        "adverse_path_comparisons": independent["adverse_path_family_comparisons"],
   104	        "covariance_comparisons": correction["covariance"]["all_family_node_comparisons"],
   105	        "edge_transport_comparisons": correction["covariance"]["matched_edge_transport_comparisons"],
   106	        "edge_transport_skipped": correction["covariance"]["skipped_edge_transport_comparisons"],
   107	        "uncertainty_bearing_covariance_points": correction["covariance"]["uncertainty_bearing_point_comparisons"],
   108	        "correction_mutation_catches": correction["exercised_mutation_catches"],
   109	        "frobenius_certification_scope": correction["frobenius_certification_scope"],
   110	        "overall_correspondence_status": "LEAD",
   111	        "maximum_conclusion": MAXIMUM,
   112	        "hashes": {
   113	            name: digest(HERE / name)
   114	            for name in (
   115	                "ATLAS_RESULT.json", "INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION_RESULT.json",
   116	                "REVIEW_CORRECTION_RESULT.json", "VERIFICATION_RESULT.json",

   123	
   124	def source_immutability() -> dict[str, object]:
   125	    observed = {}
   126	    for row in rows(HERE / "SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv"):
   127	        path = ROOT / row["path"]
   128	        if digest(path) != row["sha256"]:
   129	            raise AssertionError(f"source hash {row['path']}")
   130	        observed[row["path"]] = row["sha256"]
   131	    if len(observed) != 10:
   132	        raise AssertionError("source count")
   133	    return {"status": "PASS", "count": len(observed), "sources": observed}
   134	
   135	
   136	def prior_packages() -> dict[str, str]:
   137	    record = json.loads((PARENT / "REPOSITORY_GATES.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   138	    prior = {
   139	        row["package"]: row["manifest_sha256"]
   140	        for row in record["prior_scientific_packages"]["packages"]
   141	    }
   142	    prior[PARENT.name] = PARENT_MANIFEST
   143	    return prior
   144

   146	def main() -> None:
   147	    generic = load(
   148	        ROOT / "bootstrap_csn_phi_angular_selector_2026-07-19/verify_repository_gates.py",
   149	        "motif_hopf_generic",
   150	    )
   151	    generic.BASE = BASE
   152	    generic.PACKAGE = PACKAGE
   153	    scope = generic.validate_scope(ROOT)
   154	    scientific = scientific_results()
   155	    sources = source_immutability()
   156	    frozen = generic.validate_frozen(ROOT)
   157	    prior = prior_packages()
   158	    replay = generic.replay_packages(ROOT, prior, "PRIOR")
   159	    if len(prior) != 69 or replay["entries"] != 1864:
   160	        raise generic.GateError("PRIOR", f"{len(prior)}:{replay['entries']}")
   161	    navigation = generic.validate_navigation(ROOT)
   162	    dirty = generic.validate_dirty(ROOT, DIRTY)
   163	    tests = generic.validate_tests(ROOT)
   164	    tests.pop("stdout_sha256", None)
   165	    signature = f"{tests['passed']}|{tests['failed']}|{tests['xfailed']}|{tests['failure']}"
   166	    tests["result_signature_sha256"] = hashlib.sha256(signature.encode()).hexdigest()
   167	    package = generic.validate_package_manifest(ROOT)
   168	    catches = {
   169	        "scope": generic.expect("SCOPE", lambda: generic.validate_scope(ROOT, "LIVE.md")),
   170	        "frozen": generic.expect("FROZEN", lambda: generic.validate_frozen(ROOT, True)),
   171	        "prior": generic.expect(
   172	            "PRIOR", lambda: generic.replay_packages(ROOT, prior, "PRIOR", True)
   173	        ),
   174	        "current": generic.expect(
   175	            "NAVIGATION", lambda: generic.validate_navigation(ROOT, "current")
   176	        ),
   177	        "frontier": generic.expect(
   178	            "NAVIGATION", lambda: generic.validate_navigation(ROOT, "frontier")
   179	        ),
   180	        "dirty": generic.expect("DIRTY", lambda: generic.validate_dirty(ROOT, DIRTY, True)),
   181	        "package": generic.expect(
   182	            "PACKAGE", lambda: generic.validate_package_manifest(ROOT, True)
   183	        ),
   184	    }
   185	    output = {
   186	        "schema": "udt-motif-hopf-correspondence-repository-gates-1.0",
   187	        "base": BASE,
   188	        "result": "PASS",
   189	        "scope_paths": scope,
   190	        "scientific_verifier": scientific,
   191	        "source_immutability": sources,
   192	        "frozen": frozen,
   193	        "prior_scientific_packages": replay,
   194	        "navigation": navigation,
   195	        "dirty_checkout": dirty,
   196	        "tests": tests,
   197	        "package_manifest": package,
   198	        "catch_proofs": catches,
   199	        "compute": {"cpu_only": True, "gpu_work_performed": False},
   200	        "authority_boundary": {
   201	            "startup_controls_changed": False,
   202	            "canon_changed": False,
   203	            "action_or_equations_selected": False,
   204	            "physical_motif_selected": False,
   205	            "continuous_transport_or_dynamics_claimed": False,
   206	            "boundary_topology_or_scale_selected": False,
   207	            "carrier_or_matter_adopted": False,
   208	            "repository_reorganization_performed": False,
   209	        },
   210	    }
   211	    (HERE / "REPOSITORY_GATES.json").write_text(
   212	        json.dumps(output, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8"
   213	    )
   214	    print("repository_gates=PASS")
   215	    print(
   216	        f"scientific={scientific['coherent_identities']} identities/"
   217	        f"{scientific['family_rows']} family rows/{scientific['distribution_rows']} distributions"
   218	    )
   219	    print(
   220	        f"covariance={scientific['covariance_comparisons']} edge_transport="
   221	        f"{scientific['edge_transport_comparisons']}"
   222	    )
   223	    print(f"frozen_manifests=6 entries={frozen['entries']} paths={frozen['tracked_paths']}")
   224	    print(f"prior_packages={len(prior)} entries={replay['entries']}")
   225	    print(
   226	        f"tests={tests['passed']} passed/{tests['failed']} known failed/"
   227	        f"{tests['xfailed']} xfailed"
   228	    )
   229	    print(f"dirty_metadata_paths={dirty['paths']} hash={dirty['metadata_sha256']}")
   230	    print(f"package_manifest={package['sha256']} entries={package['entries']}")

# UDT Motif-to-Hopf Correspondence Audit

Date: 2026-07-22

Status: `CORRECTED_VERIFIED_WITH_REGISTERED_SCOPE`

Maximum conclusion:

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_REGISTERED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS`

plus

`EXACT_CONDITIONAL_RECIPROCAL-TORIC/HOPF-SEED_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS`.

The overall motif-to-Hopf correspondence remains a `LEAD`.

## Result first

The new motif vocabulary does connect to the Hopf program, but at two sharply different levels.

First, the complete registered local analytic ensemble contains abundant sampled projector motifs
and nonzero Frobenius obstruction in the registered chart. Of 95,232 instrument-family paths,
93,920 have the same classified motif and matchable projector sets at all 17 sampled nodes. This is
not a continuous-bundle theorem. At the path midpoints, 8,205 families carry the `1+1+2` motif. Its
primitive Lorentzian rank-two plane is numerically nonintegrable in 6,669 cases and integrable in
1,536 in that chart. The 1,395 four-line midpoints have three complementary rank-two splittings;
all 8,370 tested split sides are numerically nonintegrable there.

Second, in the already conditional reciprocal-toric class,

```text
g = -dt^2 + A(phi)^2 dphi^2
    + Omega(phi)^2[exp(-2phi) dxi1^2 + exp(2phi) dxi2^2],
```

the metric `phi` Hessian plus the unnormalized gradient dyad generically recovers the four intrinsic
axes `(t,phi,xi1,xi2)` without an `S2` carrier. The two angular Hessian eigenvalues differ exactly by
`2/A^2`; the dyad distinguishes depth from time. Axis recovery fails only at disclosed degeneracies
`Omega'/Omega=+/-1` unless another intrinsic instrument resolves them.

Once periodic circles, a free diagonal/anti-diagonal action, full reciprocal range, and opposite
primitive caps are separately supplied, the metric-dual connection is independent of `Omega` and
has conditional unit Hopf class. Its quotient map is exactly the same degree-one Hopf map used by
the historical `hopf_seed` code after `tan(eta)=exp(2phi)`.

This is a direct vocabulary-to-Hopf `LEAD`: the registered metric instruments exhibit local
twisting candidates, and the separately supplied reciprocal-toric specialization turns its angular
axes into the exact Hopf seed geometry. It is a geometric precursor and conditional compatibility
witness, not native carrier or matter emergence.

## Complete sampled continuation census

The scan used all

```text
4 banks * 48 carrier vectors * 16 structural masks = 3,072
```

analytic identities. Each identity was followed along its preregistered point pair at 17 affine
nodes. Every one of the 31 nonempty subsets of `R,H,D,RG,WG` was classified at every node:

```text
52,224 metric/phi two-jets
1,618,944 family classifications
95,232 family paths
```

Same-motif, matchable-projector paths at all 17 nodes:

| motif | stable paths |
|---|---:|
| full irreducible weave | 70,812 |
| scalar/silent | 11,328 |
| `1+1+2` | 7,845 |
| `1+3` | 2,880 |
| four lines | 1,055 |

The remaining 1,312 paths contain a motif transition or numerical margin. None was dropped. The
complete transition census is `FAMILY_TRANSITION_CENSUS.tsv`.

The endpoints reproduce all 190,464 corresponding rows of the frozen pointwise motif atlas with
zero classification disagreement.

These paths are coherent analytic configurations, not EOM solutions or physical evolution. Their
17 nodes establish sampled matching only. They do not establish a continuous projector bundle,
global continuation, or holonomy. Under the explicit zero-constant cubic polynomial maps defined by
the stored nonlinear jets, all `63,488` possible adjacent-edge cases were accounted for: `63,438`
admitted assignments and had zero transport discordance, while 50 were retained as mutually
unmatched transition edges. Of 67,456 point comparisons, 67,396 were classified on both sides, 33
were uncertain on one side, and 27 were uncertain on both. The node-dependent projector-set
covariance residual was at most `1.1807795359652391e-11`; the map inversion residual was at most
`1.1102230246251565e-16`, and the minimum sampled absolute Jacobian determinant was
`0.9643147372973677`.

## Local distributions

Every midpoint received complete `h=1e-4` and `h/2` four-coordinate stencils in the registered
chart. The largest derivative
convergence residual is `0.0031622520541422948`, below the preregistered `0.005` gate. Only 13
identity/family stencils are retained as degenerate or numerically uncertain; independent replay
reproduces all 13.

The main distribution observations are:

- `1+1+2`: 6,669 primitive Lorentzian planes locally nonintegrable; 1,536 integrable.
- Four lines: 8,370 complementary rank-two split sides locally nonintegrable; zero integrable.
- `1+3`: 2,879 rank-three complements locally integrable and one uncertain. This agrees with the
  hypersurface-orthogonal character expected of the nonzero `phi`-gradient dyad and reinforces that
  the gradient alone is not a generic Hopf carrier.
- Rank-one distributions are locally integrable by dimension, but remain unoriented lines.

Nonzero Frobenius obstruction is a local twist/anholonomy diagnostic. The tensor formula is valid,
but its stored normalization and numerical thresholds use registered-chart component norms; the
full census is therefore certified only in that chart. It is not a Hopf integer. No local family was assigned a
compact domain, periodicity, cap, orientation lift, or global transition cocycle; therefore all
3,072 receive `GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT`, not `Q=0`.

## Reciprocal-toric control

For the conditional toric metric, the mixed Hessian and dyad eigenvalue pairs in the coordinate
order `(t,phi,xi1,xi2)` are

```text
H: (0, -A'/A^3, (Omega'/Omega-1)/A^2, (Omega'/Omega+1)/A^2)
D: (0,  1/A^2, 0, 0).
```

Thus `H+D` as a joint instrument family distinguishes the two angular axes identically and separates
depth from time. This is generic inside that class, not universal over arbitrary positive `Omega`:
one angular line becomes degenerate with time when `Omega'/Omega=+/-1`.

The generic local ensemble supplies an important contrast. At its 3,072 `H+D` midpoints, 1,536 are
scalar, 1,530 are stably full irreducible, six are uncertain/unstable, and zero have a four-line
motif. The toric axis recovery is therefore a special commuting/cohomogeneity-one stratum, not a
generic consequence of merely turning on `H` and `D`.

With the equal-weight diagonal circle action separately supplied, the metric-dual connection is

```text
calA = f(phi) dxi1 + [1-f(phi)] dxi2,
f(phi)=1/[1+exp(4phi)].
```

`Omega` cancels. For finite endpoints,

```text
Q = f(phi_minus)-f(phi_plus),
```

so the readout is continuous and boundary-dependent, not automatically integral. Only the full
range `phi: -infinity -> +infinity`, two `2*pi` circles, opposite primitive smooth collapses,
selected free diagonal/anti-diagonal action, orientation, and normalization give `|Q|=1`.

At `phi=0` the circle fractions are equal. Reciprocal reflection exchanges the two angular
coefficients; it is a metric isometry only when `A^2` and `Omega^2` are even and the global circle
exchange is supplied. The round control has exact opposite collapse limits `(1,0)` and `(0,1)`.
Arbitrary positive `A,Omega` do not inherit periodicity or cap regularity from the local projectors.

## Comparison with the existing Hopf soliton

The quotient map is

```text
n(phi,delta) = (sech(2phi) cos(delta),
                sech(2phi) sin(delta),
               -tanh(2phi)).
```

It has unit norm and, after `tan(eta)=exp(2phi)` and `delta=xi1-xi2`, is exactly

```text
(sin(2eta) cos(delta), sin(2eta) sin(delta), cos(2eta)),
```

the degree-one Hopf map implemented by `hopf_seed` following inverse stereographic
compactification. This is exact seed-level equivalence.

It is not equality to the relaxed no-null field. The existing soliton explores deformations in an
independently posited internal `Map(S3,S2)` configuration space and is stabilized by the conditional
`L2+L4` functional. The metric audit has not derived those degrees of freedom, that action, its
coefficients, a source, time-live persistence, or mass.

## Emergence ruling

The corrected evidence supports:

`OBSERVED_BOUNDED_REGISTERED-CHART_SAMPLED_MOTIF_AND_FROBENIUS_CENSUS` and
`EXACT_CONDITIONAL_RECIPROCAL-TORIC/HOPF-SEED_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS`.

Their proposed correspondence is a `LEAD`, not a derived join.

It does not support `NATIVE_CARRIER_EMERGENCE_DERIVED`.

The remaining join is no longer simply “find an S2.” UDT would have to select or globally sustain:

1. the reciprocal-toric commuting projector stratum rather than the generic full weave;
2. periodic transverse circles and their global integral basis;
3. the diagonal/anti-diagonal free circle action and orientation;
4. opposite regular caps or an equivalent finite-cell completion;
5. a configuration space allowing metric-derived quotient textures to deform; and
6. a native reduced action/variation law whose stationary sector can be compared with the existing
   conditional soliton.

## Tile A — complete coherent-path continuation

The structural ensemble contains exactly

```text
4 analytic banks * 48 carrier vectors * 16 ensemble masks = 3,072
```

coherent analytic configuration identities. For each bank use the already registered ordered point
pair `B0:P0->P4`, `B1:P1->P5`, `B2:P2->P6`, or `B3:P3->P7`. Evaluate the same analytic metric/phi
configuration at the 17 fixed affine nodes `t=j/16`, `j=0..16` along that line.

At every node classify all 31 nonempty subsets of `R,H,D,RG,WG` with the frozen motif algorithm.
Retain every motif and margin. Match primitive projectors only by a minimum-distance assignment
between adjacent nodes after requiring identical primitive rank/signature multisets. Record
births, deaths, degeneracies, motif changes, permutation holonomy, and continuation margins. No
path is rejected for changing class.

Required coverage: 52,224 metric/phi two-jets and 1,618,944 family classifications.

These are coherent local analytic paths, not EOM solutions, worldlines, physical evolution, or a
global finite-cell atlas.

## Tile B — complete local distribution test

At each path midpoint, evaluate symmetric coordinate stencils in all four coordinates at
`h=1e-4` and `h/2`. For every one of the 31 families whose primitive projector rank/signature
multiset is stable across the stencil, match the complete projector set and estimate projector
derivatives at both steps.

For every primitive rank-two or rank-three image and every unique complementary rank-two split,
compute the projector Frobenius obstruction

```text
Q^mu_nu (P^rho_alpha nabla_rho P^nu_beta
         - P^rho_beta nabla_rho P^nu_alpha).
```

The complementary distribution is tested separately. Rank-one distributions are recorded as
locally integrable by dimension, not as globally oriented vector fields.

Numerical classification thresholds, chosen only as certification controls:

- derivative convergence `<=5e-3`: converged;
- normalized Frobenius obstruction `<=1e-7`: numerically integrable;
- obstruction `>=1e-5`: numerically nonintegrable;
- the interval between them: retained uncertain.

No local integrability result may be promoted to periodicity, topology, a physical angular sector,
or a carrier.

## Tile C — global eligibility and reciprocal-toric control

A coherent local family is eligible for a Hopf-number calculation only if its source supplies all
of the following without post-outcome choice:

1. a compact or correctly compactified three-domain;
2. a globally smooth intrinsic time/rest split or an equivalent spatial construction;
3. globally oriented projectors or an explicit transition cocycle;
4. periodic/gluing/collapse data and regular endpoint behavior;
5. an intrinsic connection with gauge/frame covariance; and
6. a normalization making the Chern-Simons/Hopf integral topological.

Absence of those data is recorded as `GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT`, not converted into a zero Hopf charge.
No coordinate cube may be silently compactified and no local polynomial coordinate may be declared
periodic.

Separately use the already disclosed conditional reciprocal-toric class as a positive algebraic
control:

```text
g = -dt^2 + A(phi)^2 dphi^2
    + Omega(phi)^2 [exp(-2phi) dxi1^2 + exp(2phi) dxi2^2].
```

`A` and `Omega` remain arbitrary positive functions on the open orbit region. The audit will derive
the `R/H/D` motif/projector structure generically, identify every degeneracy condition, and test
whether the transverse axes are recovered without using a carrier. Periods, full phi range,
diagonal/anti-diagonal circle action, and cap cycles remain separately `CONDITIONAL`; the control
must report results both with and without them.

## Tile D — connection, twist, and Hopf class

Only when the Tile-C eligibility gates are met may the metric-dual connection and its curvature be
formed. For the reciprocal-toric control, compute the general finite-endpoint Chern-Simons integral
before taking any cap limit. Report nonintegral finite-endpoint values, same-cycle/no-cap cases, both
orientations, and every discrete ambiguity. A unit class may be called conditional only after the
full registered toric/cap premises are supplied.

The metric motif projectors must not be credited with selecting the equal-weight diagonal generator
unless that selection follows from the tested geometry. If the projectors recover axes but not the
circle action, the selector remains open.

## Tile E — comparison with the existing Hopf branch

Construction remains blind to the internal `S2` field and `L2+L4` functional. After Tiles A-D are
frozen, compare any eligible metric quotient map with:

    86	def digest(path: Path) -> str:
    87	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    88	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    89	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):
